from Friday 's Daily Star
by Juan Cole
Friday , June 04 , 2004
as the american public gradually weary of the Iraq crisis , some have begin worry that the war could blow back on the US by create the condition for anti-american terrorism .
Israel , however , be much closer to Iraq and be likely to suffer from iraqi instability much more acutely than will the United States .
ironically , among the strongest proponent of war in Iraq be israeli Prime Minister Ariel Sharon and he neoconservative supporter in the US .
have they , however , actually weaken israeli security ?
the biggest threat Israel face be not from conventional army but from the asymmetrical tactic of palestinian national liberation movement .
the derailing of the Oslo peace process by the hard - line policy of Sharon and the palestinian intifada have encourage suicide bombing .
this , in turn , have discourage international investment in Israel and have make it less likely that immigrant to the country will actually remain there .
although Israel withdraw from lebanese territory in May 2000 , the radical lebanese shiite party , Hizbullah , have not be mollify .
it be estimate to have some 5,000 armed fighter , and they have pursue attack against israeli force to compel they to withdraw from the Shebaa Farms , a sliver of syrian territory that Israel annex after the 1967 war .
any thorough assessment of the impact of the Iraq war and its aftermath on Israel 's security environment must , therefore , closely examine its likely effect on the conduct of asymmetrical warfare .
although it be often allege ( without much evidence ) that Saddam Hussein give money to the family of palestinian suicide bomber and so encourage asymmetrical warfare , it be not clear that he actually pose a danger to Israel .
the Palestinians who have be willing to kill themselves to end the israeli occupation of the Gaza Strip and the West Bank be not drive by economic consideration .
Saddam never do anything practical to help the Palestinians .
at some point , as in the late 1980 , he reportedly make behind - the - scene overture to the Israelis to arrive at some sort of a deal .
he do not allow palestinian radical to launch operation against Israel from Iraq .
by the late 1990 , Iraq have no nuclear or biological weapon program , and have destroy its chemical weapon stockpile .
its ramshackle army have virtually collapse before the american invasion in 2003 .
if it be hard to see how baathist Iraq pose any real threat to Israel , it be not so difficult to see a menace in the current instability .
the bungling of post-war Iraq by the Bush administration create a weak and fail state .
armed militia , many staff by former iraqi military man with substantial training and experience , have proliferate .
the US choose to ally itself with such group as the Supreme Council for the Islamic Revolution in Iraq , whose 15,000 - strong Badr Corps paramilitary be train by the Iranian Revolutionary Guards .
anti-israeli and pro-palestinian feeling be strong among several major iraqi ideological group and current .
the more radical Shiites , who generally follow the theocratic notion of Iran 's Ayatollah Ruhollah Khomeini , routinely chant and demonstrate against Israel .
they vehemently protest the israeli assassination of Sheikh Ahmed Yassin , the leader of Hamas , last March .
worse for Israel , the assassination draw a denunciation even from the moderate and cautious Grand Ayatollah Ali Sistani , who wield enormous moral authority over iraqi Shiites .
these shiite movement have be suppress by Saddam Hussein 's regime , but have now organize and arm themselves .
they have also reestablish they historical link with lebanese and iranian Shiites .
sunni arab fundamentalist deeply sympathize with the Palestinians and with Hamas , and those in Iraq have deep historical ink with fundamentalist in Jordan and Palestine .
iraqi city such as Fallujah and Ramadi be on the truck route from Amman to Baghdad , and so come under the influence of the Salafi movement , which be popular in Jordan .
secular arab nationalist group also universally sympathize with the Palestinians , and those in post-saddam Iraq be no exception .
whereas Saddam Hussein 's dictatorship ensure that such populist current be keep firmly under control , they be now free to organize .
a Iraq in which armed fundamentalist and nationalist militia proliferate be inevitably a security worry for Israel .
if even a modicum of normality and security can be return to Iraq , its citizen will be able to benefit from the country 's petroleum reserve .
that private wealth can easily be funnel into aid for the Palestinians and for lebanese Shiites .
Israel 's security interest be best serve by peace with its neighbor , which can only be achieve by trade land for peace with the Palestinians .
Ariel Sharon 's aggressive near annexation of almost half of the occupy West Bank and he indefinite postponement of any palestinian state have create unprecedented rage and violence .
the anger have spread throughout the muslim world , include Iraq .
the promotion by the pro-zionist right of twin occupation - in the West Bank and in Iraq - have profoundly weaken , not strengthen , israeli security .
Juan Cole ( www.juancole.com ) be a professor of modern Middle East history at the University of Michigan and author of " Sacred Space and Holy War " ( I.B. Tauris , 2002 ) .
the DAILY STAR publish this commentary in agreement with Agence Global

India defensive over Sri Lanka
by Ranjit Devraj
NEW DELHI -
while India be ready to enter into a " defense cooperation agreement " with Sri Lanka , it be wary of be draw into any military involvement in the island nation 's two decade - old civil war that have see violent strife between ethnic Tamils and the sinhalese majority - leave over 60,000 dead on both side .
and that explain the delay in the signing of a formal defense agreement that be at the heart of sri lankan President Chandrika Kumaratunga 's four - day visit to India recently .
accord to Professor S D Muni , South Asia expert at the Jawaharal Nehru University , the two - year peace talk between Colombo and the Liberation Tigers of Tamil Eelam ( LTTE ) be stalemate .
" the sri lankan government do not want to initiate a conflict but would be interested in deter the LTTE from start one .
and the Tigers look as if they be on the brink of launch another offensive , " Muni tell IPS .
Colombo hold six round of talk with the Tigers between September 2002 and March 2003 .
but last April , the rebel abruptly pull out of negotiation demand recognition , first , for the right to self - rule before proceed any further .
Kumaratunga 's India tour precede a three - day visit to Sri Lanka by norwegian Foreign Minister Jan Petersen in a new bid to revive the peace talk that be suppose to follow a ceasefire that Oslo successfully broker in February 2002 .
Petersen hold discussion with both Kumaratunga and the reclusive LTTE leader Velupillai Prabhakaran in the rebel stronghold of Kilinochchi without success , and chief tamil rebel negotiator Anton Balasingham and norwegian envoy Erik Solheim hold close - door talk at the international airport late Saturday in a effort to keep the salvage effort on track , diplomatic source say .
but they , too , fail .
Colombo , too , seem to be in a intractable position .
accord to former indian army general A S Kalkat , the difficulty for Kumaratunga 's government lay in the fact that the LTTE have become a de jure power in the north and east of the island and be run every aspect of civil administration in the area within its control .
a veteran of India 's military intervention in the Jaffna peninsula to help implement the 1987 indo - Sri Lanka Peace Accord - which ambitiously provide for the disarming of the formidable LTTE - Kalkat say the new defense deal would essentially be a reiteration of the older one minus its military commitment .
" the Norwegians mean well but they role be limited to that of honest broker and the LTTE be keenly aware that they do not have the power [ unlike India ] to underwrite any arrangement , " Kalkat tell IPS in a interview .
in 1987 , the Tamil Tigers reluctantly accept the peace accord under indian pressure .
under the accord , a new northeastern provincial council be form and the indian army be deploy as peacekeeper in the north and east .
however , difference between India and LTTE soon surface and lead to clash between Tiger guerrilla and the indian peace keeping force .
about 1,200 indian soldier be kill during this phase of the conflict .
India have to pull back its force from Sri Lanka in 1989 follow the election of Ranasinghe Premadasa , a strong critic of indian mediation .
last June , a international initiative lead by Japan to persuade the LTTE to come back to the negotiating table fail despite a aid package offer of us$ 4.5 billion .
Japan 's special envoy , Yasushi Akashi , who call for tangible progress in the peace process before the money would be release , come back from visit to Colombo and Kilinochchi in early November a frustrated man .
he complain about the " visible lack of progress " and reach a impasse in talk with both side .
the Tigers 's chief ideologue , Balasingham , sniff at the proposal say that " a solution to the ethnic conflict can not be predetermine by the resolution or declaration of donor conference , but have to be negotiate by the party in conflict without the constraint of external force . "
but there be strong hint in the country that a new indo - Sri Lanka defense deal could be in the making .
and this have already draw protest from the Tamil National Alliance ( TNA ) which be back by the LTTE in the April general election hold in Sri Lanka .
" Tamils feel that the propose defense agreement between India and Sri Lanka would encourage Sinhala ruler to prepare for another war abandon the current peace process , " TNA member of parliament P Sithamparanathan be quote as say in a statement .
she add that recent visit to the island by India 's top military brass include army chief General Nirmal Chander Vij have " cause apprehension among Tamils that preparation be under way for another war in the island " .
but Kalkat point out that India would be ill - advise to be involved again , militarily , with Sri Lanka if only because it still have to consider the sentiment of 45 million ethnic Tamils in the indian state of Tamil Nadu - separate from Sri Lanka 's Jaffna peninsula by the narrow Palk Straits .
apart from the 1,200 indian life lose in 1987 , the indian peacekeeping force be immensely unpopular not only in Tamil Nadu and the Jaffna peninsula but also among the sinhalese majority who consider it a violation of they country 's sovereignty .
the best option , now , under the present difficult circumstance be for Colombo to do its own dirty work , although New Delhi can always be count on to render good neighborly help because of the share belief that religion , ethnicity and language can not be the basis for secession .
in any case , Kalkat put it succinctly : " there can not be a military option to what be a political situation . "
Asia Times Online 16/11/2004
unreport by the international media , the Valley of Kashmir have see a ethnic and cultural genocide that have result in the fleeing from the valley of almost all the hindu family who have be live there since human habitation be first record .
thus far , none of the many " human rights " busybody across the world have bother to even notice such a development .
Musharraf call the bluff
while most U.S. secretary of state -- save perhaps Dean Rusk -- have gobble up credit for outcome that they have little to do with , few have be as brazen as Colin Powell .

as Pakistan 's president have be tell the United States he be " force " into take a hawkish line on India precisely by the likes of Rahman , this be a embarrassment .

that distinction have now go to the United States .
realist , and this even include member of the U.S. democratic foreign policy establishment such as Strobe Talbott , who have long seek to divest India of its defensive capability against another nuclear power in Asia , understand the only feasible solution for Kashmir be the acceptance of the status quo .
India keep what it have while Pakistan and China ( which be gift a slice of the territory three decade ago ) do likewise .
simultaneously , New Delhi would ensure a degree of autonomy for the state that would help cut popular support off from jihadi attempt to convert Kashmir into a second Afghanistan .
this , Pakistan 's lobbyist in Washington Christina Rocca have be tell , be the " minimum " that the Pakistan army will accept .
it be also far more than what any administration in New Delhi can deliver .
this writer have for year regard the best solution to the Kashmir problem as be the trifurcation of the indian part of the state into a hindu - majority Jammu , a Buddhist - dominate Ladakh and the overwhelmingly muslim Kashmir Valley , with the third state give little of taxpayer 's money but substantial autonomy .
with luck , the Kashmir Valley can attract investment from the Middle East and other location where Muslims be dominant and become a tourist , education and service haven within India .
the overwhelming majority of Muslims in Kashmir would be happy with such a outcome , except for the tiny jihadi segment patronize by the U.S. State Department and the Pakistan Army , which would like to even the score with India for they catastrophic defeat in Bangladesh in 1971 .
unreport by the international media , the Valley of Kashmir have see a ethnic and cultural genocide that have result in the fleeing from the valley of almost all the Hindu family who have be live there since human habitation be first record .
thus far , none of the many " human rights " busybody across the world have bother to even notice such a development .
indeed , they report be fill with tale of the " atrocity " of indian troops on the innocent jihadi .
despite Sept. 11 , the United States still support the Kashmir group that back jihad as part of the price Washington be pay to keep Pervez Musharraf happy .
unfortunately for they , the general have decide to take seriously Colin Powell 's frequent boast that it be on he nudging that the Indians make conciliatory gesture toward Islamabad .
the U.S. State Department and the misname think tank that follow its lead have hold numerous conference on Kashmir and , in most of they , the solution that have emerge be a valley prize loose from indian control and under its own version of Ibrahim Rugova .
that India be not Yugoslavia and that the " foreigner - lead " Indian National Congress can least afford to ignore indian nationalism , have not strike the conferee , among whom have be several indian " scholar " and " analyst " ready to say and endorse anything for the sake of a free trip to New York or Vienna .
it be the business community in India that step in after Vajpayee indulge in a empty bout of saber rattling in 2002 , point out that the only beneficiary of the mythical perception that war -- especially nuclear war -- be around the corner in the subcontinent be China .
the reason for this be that India be emerge as a alternative investment destination to China , hence the favor that the general in Islamabad do to they trusty supplier of nuke and missile by create a scare about war involve India when in fact the real flashpoint be the Taiwan Straits and North Korea .

Bush 's National Guard year

that he do not show up for duty in Alabama ?
that he miss a physical ?
that he daddy get he in ?
news coverage of the president 's year in the Guard have tend to focus on one brief portion of that time - to the exclusion of virtually everything else .
so just for the record , here , in full , be what Bush do :
the future president join the Guard in May 1968 .
almost immediately , he begin a extended period of training .
six week of basic training .
fifty - three week of flight training .
twenty - one week of fighter - interceptor training .
that be 80 week to begin with , and there be other training period throw in as well .
it be full - time work .
by the time it be over , Bush have serve nearly two year .
not two year of weekend .
two year .
after training , Bush keep fly , rack up hundred of hour in F - 102 jet .
as he do , he accumulate point toward he National Guard service requirement .
at the time , guardsman be require to accumulate a minimum of 50 point to meet they yearly obligation .
accord to record release earlier this year , Bush earn 253 point in he first year , May 1968 to May 1969 ( since he join in May 1968 , he service thereafter be measure on a May - to - May basis ) .
Bush earn 340 point in 1969 - 1970 .
[ in other word , Bush earn enough point to satisfy the requirement for he entire six year hitch in 1969 - 1970 alone .
- acd ]
he earn 137 point in 1970 - 1971 .
and he earn 112 point in 1971 - 1972 .
the number indicate that in he first four year , Bush not only show up , he show up a lot .
do you know that ?
that bring the story to May 1972 - the time that have be the focus of so many news report - when Bush " desert " ( accord to anti-bush filmmaker Michael Moore ) or go " awol " ( accord to Terry McAuliffe , chairman of the Democratic National Committee ) .
Bush ask for permission to go to Alabama to work on a Senate campaign .
he superior officer say ok .
request like that be not unusual , say retire Col. William Campenni , who fly with Bush in 1970 and 1971 .
" in 1972 , there be a enormous glut of pilot , " Campenni say .
" the Vietnam War be wind down , and the Air Force be put pilot in desk job .
in '72 or '73 , if you be a pilot , active or Guard , and you have a obligation and want to get out , no problem .
in fact , you be help they solve they problem . "
so Bush stop fly .
from May 1972 to May 1973 , he earn just 56 point - not much , but enough to meet he requirement .
then , in 1973 , as Bush make plan to leave the Guard and go to Harvard Business School , he again start show up frequently .
in June and July of 1973 , he accumulate 56 point , enough to meet the minimum requirement for the 1973 - 1974 year .
then , at he request , he be give permission to go .
Bush receive a honorable discharge after serve five year , four month and five day of he original six - year commitment .
during he service , Bush receive high mark as a pilot .
a 1971 evaluation call Bush " a exceptionally fine young officer and pilot " who " continually fly intercept mission with the unit to increase he proficiency even further . "
and a 1972 evaluation call Bush " a exceptional fighter interceptor pilot and officer . "

+ as the implication of the Andaman Islands situation sink in , indian intelligence have inevitably come under scrutiny .
the inability to foresee in advance the assassination attempt on the pro-india political leader and former bangladeshi prime minister Sheikh Hasina Wazed last August 21 at a political rally in Dhaka , and the recent " coup " by nepalese King Gyanendra dismiss he government and impose a virtual absolute monarchy , be glaring example of intelligence failure . +
trouble on India 's island
in early February , India charge 34 arakan separatist from Myanmar with hide in the Landfall Islands , part of the Andaman Islands group ( see end note ) .
these alleged member of the Arakan Army , the military wing of the National Unity Party in Myanmar , have be charge with illegal entry .
it be likely , but not certain , that they will be deport to Myanmar .
but the news of the arakan rebel be just the tip of the iceberg when it come to grow concern in New Delhi over the security of the Andaman Islands .
report be circulate in the intelligence community that the Andaman Islands be not only thick with Myanmar rebel .
information point in this direction come to light after the December 26 tsunami , which take a heavy toll on the Andamans .
correspondent who flock in to cover the tsunami find they also have another story - the miserable security situation surround the indian navy 's Far Eastern Naval Command , now be establish along with India 's " blue water navy " .
security problem in the Andaman Sea be not new , but they have deteriorate during the past few year , in tandem with a deterioration in the security situation in Bangladesh , Nepal and Bhutan , and particularly in the northeastern indian state of Manipur , Nagaland and Tripura .
while the indian army have become rock - solid in the western front , and have develop the capability of withstand any pakistani adventure in that sector , it have become highly vulnerable in its eastern sector , where its enemy be not a national army but a multitude of secessionist , terrorist and drug - run militant operate between Southeast Asia and northeastern India through Bangladesh .
the Andaman Sea be a major conduit for this traffic , and the 572 large and small island that constitute the Andaman and Nicobar group be a natural transit base .
the drug and arm travel in all direction .
since the " Sea Tigers " of the LTTE , better know as the Tamil Tigers , be the one who rule the Andaman Sea : they carry the arm and drug for they own use and also to deliver to rebel in Aceh and all along the east coast of Africa .
it be old news that the Tamil Tigers have develop a strong network within South Africa .
this be not unknown to New Delhi .
a recent report by a journalist from Port Blair , in the Andamans , quote a unnamed official say that foreigner from Myanmar , Bangladesh and Sri Lanka have permanently settle in the island , use fake indian ration card , while citizen of Thailand , China , Indonesia and Malaysia have migrate temporarily to plunder the natural resource and leave .
" Port Blair , Havelock Islands , Diglipur , Middle Nicobar , Campbell 's Bay , Neil Islands and Rangott be mostly overrun by foreigner , " he say .
a official estimate issue in 2003 suggest there be 50,000 " foreigner " in the Andaman Islands , but unofficial figure be much higher than this .
a large number of they be Bangladeshis , who like million of they countryman have leave they densely populate homeland to settle elsewhere .
as most of they have few technical skill , and the Andamans have little demand for they in any case , they turn to smuggling and other unlawful activity .
the presence of the Sea Tigers in the area with gun , cash and drug make the situation extremely dangerous .
report from Port Blair make it evident that New Delhi get little on - the - ground intelligence , and the indian Coast Guard be grossly unequipped to deal with the surge of illegal migrant to the island .
one unnamed naval officer be quote say , " arm smuggling be a very profitable business in this region . "
consider the island 's huge strategic importance , it be amazing how lax New Delhi have be .
these island sit aside the vital sea lane of the Strait of Malacca , through which 300 tanker and merchant ship pass daily , bring in oil for the Far East and Southeast Asia .
as the implication of the Andaman Islands situation sink in , indian intelligence have inevitably come under scrutiny .
the inability to foresee in advance the assassination attempt on the pro-india political leader and former bangladeshi prime minister Sheikh Hasina Wazed last August 21 at a political rally in Dhaka , and the recent " coup " by nepalese King Gyanendra dismiss he government and impose a virtual absolute monarchy , be glaring example of intelligence failure .
with grow economic and military power , India will be dependent on smaller nation in the region increasingly to maintain regional security .
unless New Delhi do better in provide security to its own national against rebel , secessionist , drug runner and arm trafficker , it will not generate much confidence in the capital of surround nation .
in fact , it would tend to encourage more organized anti-india outfit , such as the pakistani inter- Services Intelligence ( ISI ) and outside - link Maoists , to exploit these network and weaken India 's eastern flank .
indian intelligence 's lackluster performance in deal with the LTTE be startling .
this formidable enemy , which give the indian army a black eye in the mid-1980 , have be operate in northeastern India and in the Andaman Sea for a long time .
in 2001 , accord to indian army official , security force launch a wide - range operation in the 300 - some inhabit island neighbor Andaman and Nicobar , and find huge cache of arm .
the arm be say to belong to the LTTE and " other terrorist group " .
in addition , LTTE activity in the Andaman Sea be well known to local observer .
the biggest LTTE maritime disaster be report in the now - defunct Asiaweek in 2001 .
a shipment of weapon , ammunition and explosive , believe to have be purchase from Cambodia and worth several million dollar , leave the port of Phuket in Thailand in early February 2001 aboard the freighter Comex - Joux 3 .
as be LTTE standard procedure , the vessel change its name at sea to Horizon .
on its journey across the Bay of Bengal the freighter be track by the indian navy and Orissa - base spy plane of India 's Aviation Research Center ; it be intercept by indian naval vessel off Sri Lanka 's east coast .
LTTE arm - running
in 1997 , the thai navy report the interception of a 16 - meter boat after a chase off the thai port of Ranong , and the confiscation of two ton of weapon and ammunition .
among the weapon intercept be two rocket - propel - grenade launcher , 20 assault rifle , m - 79 grenade launcher and more than 10,000 round of ammunition .
four person be arrest , reportedly belong to the Manipur Revolutionary People 's Front .
six crew member be from the Arakan region of Myanmar .
the boat be head toward Cox 's Bazar in Bangladesh .
until 1995 the LTTE maintain a base at Twante , a island off the coat of Myanmar , west of the Andaman island .
subsequently , Phuket become the LTTE 's main backup base .
a Sri Lanka - bear Tamil with a norwegian passport be arrest by thai authority in 2000 for he link with the LTTE .
at the time of he arrest , the suspect be allegedly involved in construct a " submarine " in a shipyard on the island of Sirae near Phuket on the Andaman Sea coast .
the real threat to the Andaman island be the steady building - up of port and conduit that serve the Tamil Tigers and a host of less - strong militant group .
over the past decade , Bangladesh have steadily move into a state of lawlessness .
it be widely acknowledge that the pakistani ISI have nurture a number of extremist Islamist group , such as the Harkat - ul - Jehad - al - Islami , in the port city of Chittagong , and put a number of secessionist rebel from India 's northeast in touch with this terrorist network .
a pattern of arrest and seizure indicate that arm be bring by the LTTE from Laos , Cambodia and Thailand into Chittagong , from where they be transport northward by land to Bhutan .
the route from Kalikhola in Bhutan to Cox 's Bazar pass through northern Bengal , Assam and Meghalaya , and on into Chittagong .
India 's Andaman and Nicobar Islands comprise more than 500 island lie 1,000 kilometer east of Sri Lanka in the Bay of Bengal .
stretch 750 kilometer from end to end , they reach from near the coast of Myanmar almost to Sumatra in Indonesia .
the Ten Degree Channel divide the Andamans , which be the larger and more heavily populate northern island , from the 20 or so Nicobar Islands in the south .
on South Andaman , the most heavily populate island , be Port Blair , which be the capital and the only large town in the entire archipelago .
travel to the Nicobar Islands be forbidden to non-Indians , and they be also not allow in some part of South Andaman Island .
Ramtanu Maitra write for a number of international journal and be a regular contributor to the Washington - base EIR and the New Delhi - base Indian Defense Review .
he also write for Aakrosh , India 's defense - tie quarterly journal .

Karzai , Musharraf new regional equation

that change on September 22 when President George W. Bush , Musharraf and Karzai hold a three way meeting in New York on the sideline of the UN General Assembly .

" a View from the Eye of the Storm "
talk deliver by Haim Harari at a meeting of the International Advisory Board of a large multi-national corporation , April , 2004 :
" as you know , I usually provide the scientific and technological " entertainment " in we meeting , but , on this occasion , we Chairman suggest that I present my own personal view on event in the part of the world from which I come .
I have never be and I will never be a government official and I have no privileged information .
my perspective be entirely base on what I see , on what I read and on the fact that my family have live in this region for almost 200 year .
you may regard my view as those of the proverbial taxi driver , which you be suppose to question , when you visit a country .
I could have share with you some fascinating fact and some personal thought about the israeli - arab conflict .
however , I will touch upon it only in passing .
I prefer to devote most of my remark to the broader picture of the region and its place in world event .
I refer to the entire area between Pakistan and Morocco , which be predominantly arab , predominantly moslem , but include many non-arab and also significant non-moslem minority .
why do I put aside Israel and its own immediate neighborhood ?
because Israel and any problem related to it , in spite of what you might read or hear in the world media , be not the central issue , and have never be the central issue in the upheaval in the region .
yes , there be a 100 year - old israeli - arab conflict , but it be not where the main show be .
the million who die in the Iran - Iraq war have nothing to do with Israel .
the mass murder happen right now in Sudan , where the arab moslem regime be massacre its black christian citizen , have nothing to do with Israel .
the frequent report from Algeria about the murder of hundred of civilian in one village or another by other Algerians have nothing to do with Israel .
Saddam Hussein do not invade Kuwait , endanger Saudi Arabia and butcher he own people because of Israel .
Egypt do not use poison gas against Yemen in the 60' because of Israel .
Assad the Father do not kill ten of thousand of he own citizen in one week in El Hamma in Syria because of Israel .
the Taliban control of Afghanistan and the civil war there have nothing to do with Israel .
the libyan blowing up of the Pan - Am flight have nothing to do with Israel , and I could go on and on and on .
the root of the trouble be that this entire moslem region be totally dysfunctional , by any standard of the word , and would have be so even if Israel have join the Arab league and a independent Palestine have exist for 100 year .
the 22 member country of the Arab league , from Mauritania to the Gulf States , have a total population of 300 million , larger than the US and almost as large as the EU before its expansion .
they have a land area larger than either the US or all of Europe .
these 22 country , with all they oil and natural resource , have a combine GDP smaller than that of Netherlands plus Belgium and equal to half of the GDP of California alone .
within this meager GDP , the gap between rich and poor be beyond belief and too many of the rich make they money not by succeed in business , but by be corrupt ruler .
the social status of woman be far below what it be in the Western World 150 year ago .
human rights be below any reasonable standard , in spite of the grotesque fact that Libya be elect chair of the UN Human Rights commission .
accord to a report prepare by a committee of arab intellectual and publish under the auspices of the U.N. , the number of book translate by the entire arab world be much smaller than what little Greece alone translate .
the total number of scientific publication of 300 million Arabs be less than that of 6 million Israelis .
birth rate in the region be very high , increase the poverty , the social gap and the cultural decline .
and all of this be happen in a region , which only 30 year ago , be believe to be the next wealthy part of the world , and in a moslem area , which develop , at some point in history , one of the most advanced culture in the world .
it be fair to say that this create a unprecedented breeding ground for cruel dictator , terror network , fanaticism , incitement , suicide murder and general decline .
it be also a fact that almost everybody in the region blame this situation on the United States , on Israel , on western civilization , on Judaism and Christianity , on anyone and anything , except themselves .
a word about the million of decent , honest , good people who be either devout Moslems or be not very religious but grow up in moslem family : they be double victim of a outside world , which now develop islamophobia , and of they own environment which break they heart by be totally dysfunctional .
the problem be that the vast silent majority of these Moslems be not part of the terror and the incitement , but they also do not stand up against it .
they become accomplice , by omission , and this apply to political leader , intellectual , business people and many other .
many of they can certainly tell right from wrong , but be afraid to express they view .
the event of the last few year have amplify four issue , which have always exist , but have never be as rampant as in the present upheaval in the region .
a few more year may pass before everybody acknowledge that it be a World War , but we be already well into it .
these be the four main pillar of the current world conflict , or perhaps we should already refer to it as " the undeclared World War III " :
suicide murder be not a new invention but they have be make popular , if I may use this expression , only lately .
even after September 11 , it seem that most of the Western World do not yet understand this weapon .
it be a very potent psychological weapon .
its real direct impact be relatively minor .
the total number of casualty from hundred of suicide murder within Israel in the last three year be much smaller than those due to car accident .
September 11 be quantitatively much less lethal than many earthquake
so what be all the fuss about suicide killing ?
it create headline .
it be spectacular .
it be frightening .
it be a very cruel death with body dismember and horrible severe lifelong injury to many of the wounded .
it be always show on television in great detail .
one such murder , with the help of hysterical media coverage , can destroy the tourism industry of a country for quite a while , as it do in Bali and in Turkey .
but the real fear come from the undisputed fact that no defense and no preventive measure can succeed against a determined suicide murderer .
this have not yet penetrate the thinking of the Western World .
the U.S. and Europe be constantly improve they defense against the last murder , not the next one .
we may arrange for the best airport security in the world .
but if you want to murder by suicide , you do not have to board a plane in order to explode yourself and kill many people .
who could stop a suicide murder in the midst of the crowded line wait to be check by the airport metal detector ?
how about the line to the check - in counter in a busy travel period ?
put a metal detector in front of every train station in Spain and the terrorist will get the bus .
protect the bus and they will explode in movie theater , concert hall , supermarket , shopping mall , school and hospital .
you can somewhat reduce you vulnerability by preventive and defensive measure and by strict border controls but not eliminate it and definitely not win the war in a defensive way .
and it be a war !
what be behind the suicide murder ?
money be , money and power and cold - blooded murderous incitement , nothing else .
it have nothing to do with true fanatic religious belief .
no moslem preacher have ever blow himself up .
no son of a arab politician or religious leader have ever blow himself up .
no relative of anyone influential have do it .
would not you expect some of the religious leader to do it themselves , or to talk they son into do it , if this be truly a supreme act of religious fervor ?
be not they interested in the benefit of go to Heaven ?
instead , they send outcast woman , naive child , retarded people and young incite hothead .
they promise they the delight , mostly sexual , of the next world , and pay they family handsomely after the supreme act be perform and enough innocent people be dead .
suicide murder also have nothing to do with poverty and despair .
the poorest region in the world , by far , be Africa .
it never happen there .
there be numerous desperate people in the world , in different culture , country and continent .
desperation do not provide anyone with explosive , reconnaissance and transportation .
a suicide murder be simply a horrible , vicious weapon of cruel , inhuman , cynical , well - fund terrorist , with no regard to human life , include the life of they fellow countryman , but with very high regard to they own affluent well - being and they hunger for power .
the only way to fight this new " popular " weapon be identical to the only way in which you fight organized crime or pirate on the high seas : the offensive way .
like in the case of organized crime , it be crucial that the force on the offensive be united and it be crucial to reach the top of the crime pyramid .
you can not eliminate organized crime by arrest the little drug dealer on the street corner .
you must go after the head of the " family " .
if part of the public support it , other tolerate it , many be afraid of it and some try to explain it away by poverty or by a miserable childhood , organized crime will thrive and so will terrorism .
the United States understand this now , after September 11 .
Russia be begin to understand it .
Turkey understand it well .
I be very much afraid that most of Europe still do not understand it .
unfortunately , it seem that Europe will understand it only after suicide murder arrive in Europe in a big way .
in my humble opinion , this will definitely happen .
the spanish train and the Istanbul bombing be only the beginning .
the unity of the civilized world in fight this horror be absolutely indispensable .
until Europe wake up , this unity will not be achieve .
word can be lethal .
they kill people .
it be often say that politician , diplomat and perhaps also lawyer and business people must sometimes lie , as part of they professional life .
but the norm of politics and diplomacy be childish , in comparison with the level of incitement and total absolute deliberate fabrication , which have reach new height in the region we be talk about .
a incredible number of people in the arab world believe that September 11 never happen , or be a american provocation or , even better , a jewish plot .
you all remember the iraqi Minister of Information , Mr. Mouhamad Said al - Sahaf and he press conference when the US force be already inside Baghdad .
disinformation at time of war be a accept tactic .
but to stand , day after day , and to make such preposterous statement , known to everybody to be lie , without even be ridicule in you own milieu , can only happen in this region .
Mr. Sahaf eventually become a popular icon as a court jester , but this do not stop some allegedly respectable newspaper from give he equal time .
it also do not prevent the western press from give credence , every day , even now , to similar liar .
after all , if you want to be a anti-semite , there be subtle way of do it .
you do not have to claim that the holocaust never happen , and that the jewish temple in Jerusalem never exist .
but million of Moslems be tell by they leader that this be the case .
when these same leader make other statement , the western media report they as if they could be true .
it be a daily occurrence that the same people who finance , arm and dispatch suicide murderer , condemn the act in English in front of western tv camera , talk to a world audience , which even partly believe they .
it be a daily routine to hear the same leader make opposite statement in Arabic to he people and in English to the rest of the world .
incitement by arab tv , accompany by horror picture of mutilate body , have become a powerful weapon of those who lie , distort and want to destroy everything .
little child be raise on deep hatred and on admiration of so - call martyr , and the western world do not notice it because its own tv set be mostly tune to soap opera and game show .
I recommend to you , even though most of you do not understand Arabic , to watch Al Jazeera , from time to time .
you will not believe you own eye .
but word also work in other way , more subtle .
a demonstration in Berlin , carry banner support Saddam 's regime and feature three - year old baby dress as suicide murderer , be define by the press and by political leader as a " peace demonstration " .
you may support or oppose the Iraq war , but to refer to fan of Saddam , Arafat or Bin Laden as peace activist be a bit too much .
a woman walk into a israeli restaurant in mid-day , eat , observe family with old people and child eat they lunch in the adjacent table and pay the bill .
she then blow herself up , kill 20 people , include many child , with head and arm roll around in the restaurant .
dignitary condemn the act but visit she bereaved family and the money flow .

there be numerous other example of such orwellian nomenclature , use every day not only by terror chiefs but also by western media .
these word be much more dangerous than many people realize .
they provide a emotional infrastructure for atrocity .

he be now be outperform by he successor .

the civilized world believe in democracy , the rule of law , include international law , human rights , free speech and free press , among other liberty .
there be naive old - fashioned habit such as respect religious site and symbol , not use ambulance and hospital for act of war , avoid the mutilation of dead body and not use child as human shield or human bomb .

Al Qaeda , Anthrax and Ayman : means , motive , modus operandi and opportunity
in early June 2003 , a Central Intelligence Agency ( " CIA " ) report publicly disclose that the reason for Mohammed Atta 's and Zacarias Moussaoui 's inquiry into cropduster be for the contemplate use in disperse biological agent such as anthrax .
a early September 2003 Newsweek article include a rumor by a Taliban source that at a meeting in April 2003 Bin Laden be plan a " unbelievable " biological attack , the plan for which have suffer a setback upon the arrest of Khalid Shaikh Mohammed ( " KSM " ) .
he have be capture the previous month in Rawalpindi , Pakistan .
in November 2003 , a report by a UN panel of expert conclude that Al Qaeda be determined to use chemical and biological weapon and be restrain only by technical difficulty .
in a statement issue June 16 , 2004 , the 9/11 Commission staff conclude that " Al Qaeda have a ambitious biological weapon program and be make advance in its ability to produce anthrax prior to September 11 .
accord to Director of Central Intelligence George Tenet , al Qaeda 's ability to conduct a anthrax attack be one of the most immediate threat the United States be likely to face . "
on August 9 , 2004 , it be announce that in the spring of 2001 , a man name El - Shukrijumah , also know as Jafar the Pilot , who be part of a " second wave , " have be case New York City helicopter .
photograph from a seize computer disc include the control and the lock on the door between the passenger and pilot .
in a bulletin , the FBI note that the surveillance might relate to a plot to disperse a chemical or biological weapon .
the CIA reportedly have be quietly build a case that the anthrax mailing be a international plot .
this be old news .
it be just no longer bureaucratically impolite to openly contest the FBI 's ( former ) theory about a lone , american scientist .
many people have argue that a US - base Al Qaeda operative be behind the earlier fall 2001 anthrax mailing in the US , and that the mailing serve as a threat and warning .
Princeton islamist scholar Bernard Lewis have explain that while islamist may disagree about whether kill innocent be sanction by the law of jihad , extremist like Zawahiri agree that notice must be give before biochemical weapon be use .
the letter bomb be send in connection with the detention of the blind sheik Abdel Rahman and those responsible for the earlier World Trade Center bombing in 1993 .
handwritten note and file on a laptop seize upon the capture of KSM , Al Qaeda 's # 3 , include a feasible anthrax production plan use a spray dryer and address the recruitment of necessary expertise .

the computer disk be confiscate from he during he arrest by the CIA in Azerbaijan and hand over to the egyptian authority .

this conference will examine the business and regulatory challenge to U.S. electric system in transition in effectively expand transmission capacity to meet new demand in the larger and more competitive regional market emerge under FERC 's RTO initiative .
the conference will review the parameter of these challenge and possible solution to they .
it will examine technology option and new business model for transmission expansion .
it will analyze emerge proposal for effective transmission planning and pricing , include market - base pricing alternative to FERC 's traditional pricing method .
the conference will also discuss what it will take in legislative action and regulatory initiative to achieve a efficient regime for ensure that the nation have a reliable grid and regional trading system .
the brochure for the Conference and associated Workshops can be obtain by click on the link below : < http://www.euci.com/pdf/trans_expn.pdf > << http://www.euci.com/pdf/trans_expn.pdf >>

for Curr LME LME ( Spot ) 01 Mar 01 jpy / usd
a currency transaction with Enron Europe Finance & Trading Limited ( " EEFTL " ) as agent for Risk Management & Trading Corp. under which either ( a ) for the case in which counterparty submit a offer to buy from EEFTL , counterparty shall receive the base currency amount and shall pay the foreign currency amount , or ( b ) for the case in which counterparty submit a offer to sell to EEFTL , counterparty shall pay the base currency amount and shall receive the foreign currency amount .

the settlement date shall be the date ( s ) set forth in the product description on the website .
the price be quote in jpy ( the ' foreign currency ' ) per US dollar ( the ' base currency ' ) .

as you know , the suffix online be purely descriptive and now use by many company .
therefore , any trade mark registration that incorporate the word online as a suffix in the way that you use it will not enable its owner to prevent other from use the word online .
give the above , if you have adequate protection for the word ENRON ( which cover the service that you offer on - line as well as you core activity ) , I would say that another application for the word ENRON ONLINE be probably unnecessary .

12/21/2000 07:50 pm
confidential settlement document per CPUC rule 51
gas accord ii settlement participant :
attach be PG&E 's gas accord ii ( ga ii ) settlement proposal .
we believe it address many of the issue and concern you have raise in the workshop .
as a overview , this proposal : * maintain the basic gas accord structure in place today for the period 2003 to 2007 . *
* offer end user transportation rate for 2003 lower for most customer than rate in effect today . *
* provide for vintage redwood path rate for core customer . *
* offer a 7.5 cent / dth rate to large customer while minimize rate change to other customer , minimize the incentive for these customer to seek to bypass local transmission charge and other CPUC - approve charge . *
* adopt guideline to improve reliability and help moderate price in gas commodity market , and identify the capital project need to meet these guideline over the course of the ga ii period ( 2003 - 2007 ) . *
* provide a high degree of rate stability , with a 3.5 % escalator to capture both inflation and the cost of need capital project .
the guarantee rate will be adjustable only for significant change in the cost of capital or increase cost due to governmental requirement or catastrophic event . *
* preserve a rate differential between the redwood and baja path , although somewhat less than the current differential . *
* propose a two - stage open season for firm transportation service begin in 2003 , with end user receive a first option on available capacity . *
* maintain the core aggregation program with some adjustment .
PG&E also anticipate that the core procurement incentive mechanism ( cpim ) will be similar to today 's mechanism , but will reflect the somewhat larger capacity holding need to meet anticipate increase in core demand and to meet a 1 - day in 10 - year cold weather event .
this also will serve as a reminder that a all - party meeting be schedule at PG&E 's headquarters in San Francisco on January 10 and 11 , to discuss this proposal and to respond to you question .
we look forward to answer you question and receive you feedback .
the attach document include the ga ii settlement proposal , a attachment ( a copy of PG&E 's propose gas rule 27 ) , and a set of support workpaper .
finally , please note that the settlement document and the attachment be in " Word 2000 " format .
we would be glad to provide the same document in a earlier version of Word , upon request by individual party .
we look forward to see you on January 10 - 11 .
in the meantime , we extend we best wish for a safe and happy holiday season .
Frank Lindh Ray Williams ( 415 ) 973-2776 ( 415 ) 973-3634

instead of suggest a specific rate increase - 10 or 15 % , I think we should acknowledge that a " modest " increase may be necessary and may in fact be desirable - but that the specific amount of increase should be reasoned and subject to well think out evidence and hearing , not just determine by whim .
in general , we should not be overly prescriptive at this point and I know you agree with that .
otherwise , I think you have capture the point excellently .
we be in the process of develop a strategy to take we through the next few month .
observation -- the pressure to finger somebody for " price gouging " be increase .
the administration be hell bent on find a " fall guy . "
the price spike pose real political risk for Davis and he and he folk need and want a easy way out .
he press release follow the hearing renew the call for " refund . "
on my panel , Loretta Lynch ask Reliant and Duke to supply she with the detail of the contract they cut to sell they power forward to marketer .
and Carl Wood 's remark be extreme .
at the Barton hearing , a liberal democrat ( Filner ) and a conservative Republican ( Hunter ) lock arm in call for refund .
Bilbray join the " gouging " band wagon .
the utility repeatedly call on FERC to do a " real " investigation , with hearing , testimony , data discovery --- the work .
on the positive side , the FERC commissioner laud Wolak , he analysis , and he remark on the panel .
Wolak say somewhat emphatically that the nature of California 's market structure make it impossible to single out a single participant as the culprit .

probe the ' palace coup '
electricity : a panel focus on price hike and the action of the ISO president .
September 26 , 2001
by KIMBERLY KINDY
the Orange County Register
a state Senate committee be set today to start serve 16 subpoena on electricity producer and official who manage California 's energy grid to determine whether they act in concert to manipulate energy price .
the investigative committee , head by state Sen. Joe Dunn , D - Santa Ana , be focus on a series of event last fall fill with enough shakespearean plot twist and intrigue that it have earn a name around the Capitol : " the palace coup . "
lawmaker and consumer group allege that the event - direct by the man who head the state 's energy grid - fuel the California energy crisis , push the state into the power - buy business and help make billion of dollar for power producer .
the central question behind the palace coup be whether Terry Winter , the president of the Independent System Operator , act alone when he take step to remove key price cap design to limit the amount power generator could charge .
Winter defy he own board and Gov. Gray Davis when he file a 50 - page request to remove the cap , record and interview show .
" I do not know how these event could have take place without some concerted effort , " say Dunn .
the subpoena will force those involve , include Winter , to provide swear testimony about the event to the committee , and to turn over e-mail , personal calendar and memo .
Davis spokesman Steve Maviglio say the governor feel " betrayed " by the action of Winter .
" the governor believe it be the define moment , when what be a mount problem turn into a instant crisis , " Maviglio say .
Winter refuse comment , refer all question to the public relation office .
ISO spokesman Gregg Fishman say Dunn 's committee will find no criminal conduct .
the decision be make by ISO upper management with one goal in mind : to keep the light on .
at the time , generator be refuse to sell power in California because of the price cap .
" it be a emergency , " Fishman say .
" we have to take action . ''
what become known as the palace coup begin on Oct. 26 when ISO board member vote for severe restriction on the amount of money electricity producer could charge for power .
" they ( electricity generator ) grin and bear the $ 750 price cap , but this new plan by ISO be too much , " say Dunn , whose committee have be investigate since March .
" all hell break loose . ''
record show that on Oct. 31 , power generator and electricity trader file letter with the Federal Energy Regulatory Commission , demand that the new plan be kill .
the letter , six in all , be send within two hour of each other and represent dozen of power generator .
" if not remove immediately , the ( ISO ) price cap will sow confusion in the market , threaten reliability and stifle new investment in generating capacity , '' read one letter write by Duke Energy vice president William Hall iii .
although there be nothing illegal about the generator act together to lobby against price cap , Dunn believe the letter and other action around the same time show clear coordination among energy official .
he say the main aim of the subpoena will be to determine whether collusion occur to " fix " price , which would violate federal trade law .
in the Oct. 31 letter , electricity producer tell federal official that if price cap be not remove it would lead to a collapse of the energy market .
the generator get they way .
the next day , the federal commission kill the new pricing plan .
what be leave in place be a $ 250 price cap establish five month earlier .
power producer then turn they attention toward kill that cap , say they could not make a profit even under these constraint .
they begin to withhold power from California , and on Dec. 7 the ISO declare its first stage 3 emergency and brace for blackout , which be narrowly avert .
what follow the next day be consider by the governor and Dunn to be the pivotal moment of the energy crisis .
Winter , who in he position as president and chief operate officer of the ISO , submit a 50 - page emergency request , ask federal official to abolish the $ 250 price cap .
final authority over lift the cap rest with the federal government .
neither the ISO board , which have establish the price cap , nor the governor learn of Winter 's action until the cap have be remove .
in fact , the attorney who help draft the emergency request , Charles Robinson , be in a meeting with representative of the governor and ISO board member just hour before the filing be make .
he do not mention anything about it .
" in retrospect , we should have tell they , '' Robinson say .
" the ISO staff sit in a meeting with the governor 's key energy adviser with poker face , not say a word about something that be go on at the exact same moment , '' Maviglio say .
" it be beyond belief that they fail to mention something so significant .
this action accelerate the utility 's move toward bankruptcy and force the governor to move the state into the power - buy business . "
price for electricity jump from a average of $ 249 a megawatt to $ 700 a megawatt within three day , ISO record show .
Dunn believe the result overcharge for electricity exceed $ 30 billion .
Robinson say the filing - grant two hour after the request - help rather than hurt Californians .
price , he say , do not spike as a result .
instead they follow the skyrocket price of natural gas - which be use to run power plant to generate electricity .
Robinson say the emergency order allow the ISO to secure refund should overcharge for electricity be prove to federal official .
" we believe the action we take address a severe concern , '' Robinson say .
" in we view , we do not believe we change or make worse the financial situation .
we feel we make it better because it introduce a process for review and refund . "
Jan Smutney - Jones , who be the ISO board chairman at the time and executive director of a group that represent power generator , say Winter do not consult he about eliminate the price cap .
Smutney - Jones also say he be unaware of anyone in the power - generating community be consult .
" Terry do this by himself , '' say Smutney - Jones , executive director of the Independent Energy Producers .
" he do what he think have to be do at the time to keep the power flow . "
the ISO board call a emergency meeting the next week demand Winter explain he action .
some board member push to have Winter remove , but there be concern such action would lead to more chaos , the governor 's spokesman Maviglio say .
James J. Hoecker , the former Federal Energy Regulatory Commission chairman , defend make the December decision and also defend Winter .
" they file a emergency motion , and we be not about to let California go dark , '' Hoecker say .
" they ( ISO management ) do what any independent system operator would do . "
what Dunn 's committee hope to learn be why all these event transpire .
he believe memo and e-mail around the time of Winter 's Dec. 8 action should provide vital clue .
" we do not know why he do what he do , but we be eager to find out , " Dunn say .
" Terry say he make that filing in the interest of Californians , but I find that argument have no basis in fact . ''
we should resurrect Mike Smith 's note and get he on the call in the attempt to avoid recreate the wheel on this one .
I can dig it up if you would like .

Quebecker win U.S. bravery award
a Quebec man be award a Carnegie Medal for bravery on Monday for save two friend by fight off a polar bear with a pocket knife two year ago on Baffin Island
" all of the research and all of the preparation I do lead up to the trip give no indication that there be bear in the Soper [ River ] valley where we be canoe , " Dr. Fortier say .
Dr. Fortier , a orthodontist , learn there be at least one polar bear in the central region of Baffin Island in July 2001 when he feel what he think be a dog lean on he tent wall .
" my first thought be to push it away , " he say .
" a few seconds later my girlfriend see the shadow of a bear 's paw through the tent fly and then it start rip through the ceiling . "
the polar bear be more dangerous than most other bear .
the latter usually consider human being a threat but the polar bear consider human a snack , expert say .
the two scream to frighten the bear and warn they friend in a tent several metre away but the bear rip into that tent and begin maul 31 - year - old Alain Parenteau .
" they scream change , " Dr. Fortier say .
" I grab my glass and my knife and unzip my tent and head out . "
the bear dwarf the 6 - foot - 1 Mr. Parenteau , knock he to the ground , he say .
Dr. Fortier throw a large rock at the bear , distract it and allow Parenteau to escape but it then turn on 25 - year - old Patricia Doyon , who be in the same tent .
again Dr. Fortier throw rock at the bear and again its target be able to escape .
" the bear give chase and I give chase , " he say .
" at some point , Patricia trip or the bear trip she and be at she back .
I be beside the bear 's head and I stab it with a upper cut below the jaw in the neck a couple of time . "
the bear run off .
while there be some fur and blood on the nine - centimetre blade , Dr. Fortier say he do not think he hurt the bear badly .
both Mr. Parenteau and Ms. Doyon , however , be bleed badly .
Dr. Fortier and he girlfriend lash two canoe together and paddle eight kilometre along the Soper River .
Dr. Fortier travel another three kilometre by foot to seek help in the nearest settlement .
both Mr. Parenteau and Ms. Doyon be airlift to a hospital and survive , though Mr. Parenteau have a gash within a centimetre of he jugular , Dr. Fortier say .
Dr. Fortier be one of 15 people to receive the Carnegie Medal on Monday .
the bronze medal be give to people who " risk they life to a extraordinary degree while save or attempt to save the life of other . "
the other canadian recipient of the medal be Ronald Joseph Crawford , 42 , of Hamilton , who be kill Aug. 4 , 2002 , while try to defend a Hamilton sandwich shop owner from a robber wield a knife .
Mr. Crawford throw several punch at the assailant before he be stab in the heart .
U.S. industrialist Andrew Carnegie start a hero fund in 1904 after be inspire by rescue story from a mine disaster that kill 181 people .
the award come with a $ 3,500 ( U.S. ) grant .
important information of big company
it be the favorite fruit of founder Steve Jobs .
he be three month late in file a name for the business , and he threaten to call he company Apple Computers if the other colleague do not suggest a better name by 5 o'clock .
it be not a acronym as popularly believe .
it be short for San Francisco .
the name be derive from the founder 's name Dr. Michael Cowpland .
it stand for COwpland REsearch Laboratory .
the name start as a joke boast about the amount of information the search - engine would be able to search .
it be originally name ' Googol ' , a word for the number represent by 1 follow by 100 zero .
after founder - Stanford graduate student Sergey Brin and Larry Page present they project to a angel investor , they receive a cheque make out to ' Google '
founder Jack Smith get the idea of access e-mail via the web from a computer anywhere in the world .
when Sabeer Bhatia come up with the business plan for the mail service , he try all kind of name end in ' mail ' and finally settle for hotmail as it include the letter " html " - the programming language use to write web page .
it be initially refer to as HoTMaiL with selective uppercasing .
Bill Hewlett and Dave Packard toss a coin to decide whether the company they found would be call Hewlett - Packard or Packard - Hewlett .
Bob Noyce and Gordon Moore want to name they new company ' Moore Noyce ' but that be already trademark by a hotel chain so they have to settle for a acronym of integrated electronics .
Lotus ( Notes )
Mitch Kapor get the name for he company from ' the lotus position ' or ' padmasana ' .
Kapor use to be a teacher of Transcendental Meditation of Maharishi Mahesh Yogi .
coin by Bill Gates to represent the company that be devoted to microcomputer software .
founder Paul Galvin come up with this name when he company start manufacture radio for car .
the popular radio company at the time be call Victrola .
Larry Ellison and Bob Oats be work on a consulting project for the CIA ( Central Intelligence Agency ) .
the code name for the project be call Oracle ( the CIA see this as the system to give answer to all question or something such ) .
the project be design to help use the newly write sql code by IBM .
the project eventually be terminate but Larry and Bob decide to finish what they start and bring it to the world .
they keep the name Oracle and create the RDBMS engine .
later they keep the same name for the company .

answer by : googlenut - ga on 25 Oct 2004 19:14 pdt
hello yheggy - ga ,
on September 21 , 2004 , the U.S. Senate Appropriations Committee approve $ 16.379 billion in funding for NASA for fiscal year 2005 .
this be a $ 200 million increase over what NASA receive for fiscal year 2004 .
U.S. Senate Committee on Appropriations
September 21 , 2004
" National Aeronautics and Space Administration ( NASA ) : be fund at $ 16.379 billion , a increase of $ 200 million over the fy04 enact level , and a reduction of $ 665 million from the budget request .
a additional $ 800 million in emergency funding be add for NASA during the committee 's consideration of the bill .
-- the return to flight activity for the shuttle program be fund at $ 4.319 billion , the request level from the administration .
-- the International Space Station be fund at $ 1.6 billion .
the bill reduce ISS operation by $ 120 million due to the continue reduce capability of the ISS for at least half of fy05 .
-- the Moon / Mars vision :
--- the Crew Exploration Vehicle ( CEV ) be fund at $ 268 million .
--- a lunar exploration mission be fund at $ 20 million .
--- $ 10 million be provide for Centennial Challenges .
Neighborhood Reinvestment Corporation ( NRC ) : be fund at $ 115 million , the same as fy04 and the budget request . "
Senate increase NASA fund
" the Senate Appropriations Committee use a somewhat controversial technique Tuesday to increase NASA 's fiscal year 2005 budget by $ 200 million over what President Bush request .
the committee vote to give NASA $ 16.4 billion in 2005 , about $ 200 million more than what the President request and over $ 1 billion more than what House appropriator approve in July . "

by Richard Spencer
( file : 19/11/2004 )
China 's insatiable demand for energy be prompt fear of financial and diplomatic collision around the globe as it seek reliable supplies of oil from as far away as Brazil and Sudan .
a intrusion into japanese territorial water by a chinese nuclear submarine last week and a trade deal with Brazil be the latest apparently unconnected consequence of China 's soar economic growth .
increase car usage in China be create a high demand for petrol
the connection , however , lie in a order issue last year by President Hu Jintao to seek secure oil supplies abroad - preferably one which could not be stop by America in case of conflict over Taiwan .
the submarine incident be put down to a " technical error " by the chinese government , which apologise to Japan .
but even before the incident the People 's Daily , the government mouthpiece , have comment that competition over the East China Sea between the two country be " only a prelude of the game between China and Japan in the arena of international energy " .
the west , however , have pay little attention to these development .
for the United States and Europe be far more concerned with the even more sensitive issue of China 's relation with " pariah state " .
in September , China threaten to veto any move to impose sanction on Sudan over the atrocity in Darfur .
it have invest $ 3 billion in the african country 's oil industry , which supply it with seven per cent of its need .
then , this month , it say that it oppose move to refer Iran 's nuclear stand - off with the International Atomic Energy Agency to the United Nations Security Council .
a week before , China 's second biggest state oil firm have sign a $ 70 billion deal for oilfield and natural gas development with Iran , which already supply 13 per cent of China 's need .
China have its own reserve of oil and natural gas and once be a net oil exporter .
but as its economy have expand by a average of nine per cent per year for the last two decade , so have its demand for energy .
this year it overtake Japan as the world 's second largest consumer of energy , behind the US .
its project demand , boost by a huge rise in car ownership as well as the need to find alternative to pollute coal for electricity generation , have contribute to the surge in the price of oil this year .
shortage be already lead to power cut in the big city .
since President Hu order state - own oil firm to " go abroad " to ensure supply , they have begin drill for gas in the East China Sea , just west of the line that Japan regard as its border .
Japan protest , to no avail , that the project should be a joint one .
the two be also set to clash over Russia 's oil wealth .
Japan favour a route to the sea , enable oil to be ship to both Japan and China .
China want a overland route through its own territory , which would give it ultimate control if hostility break out .
increasingly , analyst be say that China 's effort have go beyond what be safe or even in its own interest .
Claude Mandil , the executive director of the International Energy Agency in Paris , say the reserve in the East China Sea be hardly worth the trouble .
" nobody think that there will be a lot of oil and gas in this part of the world , " he say .
" it may be a difficult political issue but I do not think the energy content be worthwhile . "
" if China 's economy falter , which , in my view , appear increasingly likely , then commodity price will plummet , and with they , the value of the asset that produce they , " Jason Kindopp , Eurasia 's lead China analyst , say .
" Beijing may end up in a early 1990 Japan situation , where it be force to sell recently purchase overseas asset for a fraction of what it pay for they . "
China 's wider aggression to secure oil and gas be the greatest threat to its international standing in the next decade .
" Sudan be the primary example , " he say .
" it mark the first time in recent year that China have promise to wield its veto power in the UN Security Council against a petition initiate by the United States and back by France and Great Britain . "
