visualization as a helpful begin technique
if you consider that you still need the assistance of other visualization to help the mind feel the spirit of transcendence , try the follow before move onto the more formal method below .
visualisation can be as useful tool , but meditation be more than that .
meditation have to do with what be call ideation .
it be always good to stick to a formal intense meditation practice like the one for beginner describe in the mp3 file that follow after the visualisation .
find a comfortable place on the floor and sit with you leg cross .
you breathing should be calm and relaxed , through the nose .
spend a minute or so concentrate on you breath , feel the air flow through you nostril .
1 . warm sun visualization
continue to breathe slowly and deeply .
with each breath , feel the muscle in you body become lighter and lighter , and also you external motor and sensory organ be feel like they be withdraw from the world into a special inner quietness .
imagine the tension melt away as you continue breathe rhythmically and naturally .
picture yourself sit on a warm , tropical beach bask in the glow of the sun ... .
visualize the vivid , beautiful colour of the earth ( its flower and plant ) , the sea next to you , and the sky above you .
feel yourself float above the earth and sea .
as you sit above the world , the warmth of the golden sun penetrate you body and make you feel warmer and warmer .
it surround you .
the golden ray feel soft and soothing .
now you be far above the earth - into space .
everything around you be so vast .
yet , there be warmth and a familiarity with the vastness .
you want to merge you mind with the greater universal mind that surround you .
continue to ideate on this intense desire for you mind to merge with the that universal consciousness .
and while do so continue use the baba nam kevalam mantra ( breathe in with baba nam , breathe out with kevalam ) .
try this for 5 to 10 minute .
now come back to earth again - slowly .
imagine yourself sit on the beach serenely and restfully .
you muscle be loose and limp .
feel you body sink slightly into the sand make that earthly connection again .
the sun 's ray and warmth be still with you , surround you .
you be in a state of peace and relaxation .
with each breath , watch you body and ensure that it remain relaxed - at peace .
continue to feel the warmth of the sunlight all over you body , warm you deeply and gently .
you want to bring something back with you from you deep space experience where you sense you mind merge with the universal mind .
this will be the warmth of the sun - a close reminder and link between earth and the infinite space .
visualize the inside of you body bath in the golden light , absorb every ray and glow as radiantly as the sun .
a warm , gentle breeze swirl around you body and relax you even more .
let you mind and body be totally at peace .
now feel yourself return to where you sit ... move you hand and foot a little , stretch they .
open you eye .
2 . mountain visualization
another thing you can try .
imagine you be sit on top of a mountain , and that it be the most peaceful place you can think of .
feel that you be sit there in complete peace , right on top of the world .
now imagine that infinite happiness be surround you in every direction .
feel you be completely surround by that infinite peace and happiness .
now start to repeat within you mind the mantra : baba nam kevalam .
its meaning be " infinite happiness be everywhere " .
feel the meaning , do not just think of its wordy meaning or try to translate from Sanskrit ( baba nam kevalam ) to a english meaning ( infinite peace and happiness ) .
think internally , intuitively , not by word , of the meaning , as you be repeat it .
this be call ideation .
it be important to take the idea , not just the intellectual analysis .
touch deep into the idea be what build intuition - it be a synthetic process .
whereas , try to translate and grapple with wordy meaning be a intellectual mechanism - a analytical process .
feel you be surround by infinite peace and happiness , and feel that you own sense of existence be in direct contact with that endless peace and happiness all around you .
you can go further and feel that you unit consciousness , a dot in the infinite consciousness , be merge with infinity .
ok that be fairly basic :) .
the important point be to develop some psycho-spiritual connection between you mind and the universal consciousness or supreme consciousness .
do not worry if you have trouble concentrate on the mantra and ideation - that be normal .
it take some time and practice to be able to focus on the one thought .
the main thing be to keep practice .
if you do not practice , then nothing happen .
well maybe a miracle could happen , but let s face it we be ordinary people and so require practical day to day technique !
NORTH CAROLINA RELIGIOUS COALITION for MARRIAGE EQUALITY
from what we hear from the news media , one could easily conclude that all Christians be opposed to gay marriage .
but that be not the case .
last year a organization name the North Carolina Religious Coalition for Marriage Equality be form to get out the message that at least some people of faith be not opposed to extend the rights and responsibility of civil marriage to same - gender couple .
it present the case for marriage equality and state , " we be resolve that the State should not interfere with same - gender couple who choose to marry and share fully and equally in the rights , responsibility , and commitment of civil marriage . "
a measure to amend the NC constitution to ban gay marriage be defeat last year but already have be reintroduce in the 2005 legislative session , so there be a real need for visible support for the " pro-same - gender - marriage " side of this issue .
at its February meeting the CHS Vestry vote unanimously to add they name to the declaration .
we rector Barbara and we deacon Clare also have sign the declaration .
furthermore , the Vestry vote unanimously to invite the support of member of the CHS congregation for the declaration .
( since the declaration be write as come from " religious leader , " people who do not consider themselves " religious leader " can sign as " supporter of the North Carolina Religious Coalition for Marriage Equality . " )
please note that the declaration address only civil marriage ; it say nothing about religious belief or practice regard marriage .
if you have any question please feel free to call I ( after Sat. the 26th , when I will return from a trip ) .
sign - up list will be available at the service on Feb. 27 and March 6 , or you can email I .
I will email name and email address ( or postal address ) of signer to NCRC4ME in time for they " lobby day " in Raleigh on March 15 .
thank you for you consideration of this issue .
for the Church of the Holy Spirit Vestry ,
Dudley Cate 828-296-8466 jodud...@aol.com
North Carolina Religious Coalition for Marriage Equality declaration of religious leader April 19 , 2004
the most fundamental human right , after the necessity of food , clothing and shelter , be the right to affection and the supportive love of other human being .
we can grow in we capacity to be human - to be loving - in a family unit .
this right to love and form a family be so fundamental that we United States Constitution take it for grant in its dedication to " secure the blessing of liberty to ourselves and we posterity . "
the North Carolina Constitution likewise affirm the " inalienable rights " of human being to " life , liberty , the enjoyment of the fruit of they own labor , and the pursuit of happiness . "
throughout history , tyrant have know that by deny the right of oppress people to form and nurture family , they can kill the spirit of those people .
> from the shameful history of slavery in America , the injustice of forbid people to marry be evident as a denial of a basic human right .
the american law forbid interracial marriage , now strike down , be clearly discriminatory .
denial of the status of marriage to those who would freely accept its responsibility create legal and economic inequity and social injustice .
we feel call to protest and oppose this injustice .
as religious people , clergy and lay leader , we be mandate by faith to stand for justice in we common civic life .
we oppose the use of sacred text and religious tradition to deny legal equity to same - gender couple .
as concerned citizen we affirm the liberty of adult of the same gender to love and marry .
we respect the fact that debate and discussion continue in many of we religious community as to the scriptural , theological and liturgical issue involve .
however , we draw on we many faith tradition to arrive at a common conviction .
we be resolve that the state should not interfere with same - gender couple who choose to marry and share fully and equally in the rights , responsibility , and commitment of civil marriage .
we affirm freedom of conscience in this matter .
likewise , a denial of state civil recognition dishonor the religious conviction of those community and clergy who officiate at , and bless , same - gender marriage .
the state may not favor the conviction of one religious group over another by deny individual they fundamental right to marry and to have those marriage recognize by civil law .
as faith leader , we commit ourselves to public action , visibility , education , and mutual support in the service of the right and freedom to marry .
Tom Dempsey Gulf Breeze , FL 850-748-0740

he have a long and distinguished record , include many year as a federal appeal judge , the next level below Supreme Court .
he have encyclopedic knowledge of hundred of different Supreme Court case , and he can recite detail from memory .

he co-worker love he .
he fellow judge love he .
he family love he .
President Bush love he .
yes , it be true that some people do not like the way they think he will vote on the Supreme Court .

China launch its second manned spaceflight mission
secretive effort keep outsider in the dark about the program 's goal
by MARK CARREAU
copyright 2005 Houston Chronicle
China launch Shenzhou VI , its second manned spacecraft , early today in northwest China 's Gansu Province .
a pair of military pilot embark on China 's second manned space flight early today , hurtle into orbit on a test mission that could span five day .
the crew of the Shenzhou VI spacecraft be identify as Fei Junlong , 40 , and Nie Haishen , 41 , by China 's official news agency .
the successful launch from the Jiuquan Satellite Launch Center in northwest China follow the solo flight of Yang Liwei in October 2003 .
he one - day mission vault he communist homeland into the elite circle of spacefaring nation - Russia and the United States - that can launch and sustain human in space .
most expert believe China intend to develop a small space station of its own over the next several year .
President Bush have direct NASA to return to the moon by 2018 with a new generation of human explorer .
China 's " be not a fly - by - night program , " say Joan Johnson - Freese , a expert on national security who follow space development in the asian nation at the Naval War College in Newport , R.I .
" they be not in any hurry .
they want a program that will be a success , " Johnson - Freese say .
" they be not go to rush it , because they do not want it to be a budget buster .
economics will be a big determiner in the speed of they program . "
China 's overture to join the U.S. - lead effort to develop the 16 - nation international space station have be thwart for more than a decade over a range of issue , include the asian country 's human rights policy and worry it could acquire technology that could pose a security threat .
the freeze thaw some after Yang 's 2003 mission .
China be among 30 nation invite to send a delegate to NASA - sponsor roundtable discussion on Bush 's strategy to reach the moon with astronaut as the first step in the exploration of Mars and other - deep space destination .
" we applaud China 's space achievement , " NASA spokesman Allard Beutel say Tuesday .
" we wish they a successful return of they astronaut . "
he stress , however , that NASA would not follow this week 's chinese mission through formal channel .
at present , there be no plan for additional meeting with foreign power to discuss the Bush exploration initiative or to extend a invitation to China to join the space station partnership , Beutel say .
the flight of Fei and Nie could mark the end of the open chapter in a three - phase chinese space initiative , Johnson - Freese say .
the first phase , she say , will demonstrate the capability of a multi-compartment spacecraft that will leave a test module in orbit when the two flier return to Earth .
the chinese program 's second phase will include spacewalk on future mission and demonstration of docking and undocking technique .
the final phase will feature the assembly and operation of a longer - duration space lab .
at least one expert believe China 's intention might include a surprise attempt to circle the moon with astronaut before NASA 's plan lunar return .
" there be always the possibility they could jam we up , make we look like we be not numero uno , " Pike say .
during the U.S. and russian lunar race during the Cold War , NASA score a early coup by circle the moon with the Apollo 8 crew over the 1968 Christmas holiday .
as it turn out , the Soviets never make it to the moon .
" ( China ) could be the second country to do that , " Pike say .
" they would get in line in front of the Russians .
and they would not have to land on the moon to take we down a notch . "
Pike 's concern be base on China 's development of a new medium - lift rocket , the Long March V , and the construction of a new space launch complex on Hainan Island in the South China Sea .
the two development , he say , could eventually enable China 's space program to mature to the point that expert could assemble and launch from Earth 's orbit a spacecraft capable of circle the moon with astronaut and return home .

Blue Planet : who be afraid of Big Bad Wolf ?
by Dan Whipple
UNITED PRESS INTERNATIONAL
Boulder , CO , Feb. 23 ( UPI ) --
ever since he eat up Red Riding Hood 's grandma and blow down the house of two - third of the Three Little Pigs , the Big Bad Wolf have hold a persistently bad reputation .
in part because of that reputation , the gray wolf be nearly exterminate from the lower 48 state by the 1920 , except for a small remnant population on Isle Royale National Park in Michigan 's Lake Superior .
the last wolf be kill in Yellowstone National Park in 1943 .
western sheep and cattle rancher , on whose behalf this extermination campaign be conduct , gratefully dust they hand of the wolf and write he off as a job well do .
they sheep could graze , they cow could ruminate and never a discouraging word would be hear .
after the major kill - off , wolf outside of Alaska and Canada exist mostly as legend .
like ufo or Sasquatch , several people claim to see fleeting lone wolf , usually in Yellowstone .
in the 1960 , a group shoot a movie in the Wyoming park reportedly import some captive wolf , then release they when they shooting be done .
if so , this happy band have not be hear from since .
rumor also have it some renegade biologist bring a cage pair to Yellowstone and release they into the wild sometime in the 1970 , hope to reestablish a breed population .
if true , the caper fail .
over time , the wolf 's absence seem to rehabilitate its image .
eventually , a trickle of support appear for bring the predator back to its former home range in the northern Rocky Mountains .
this trickle grow into a flood , result in 14 wolf be reintroduce in Yellowstone in 1995 by the U.S. Fish and Wildlife Service -- albeit over the strong and still - continue objection of rancher .
these wolf pack have flourish , and now there be a estimate 850 wolf roam the northern Rockies , where merely 10 year ago there be none .
one compelling argument for reintroduction be the wolf act as a keystone predator , a animal that affect the population , behavior and ecology of a wide variety of species within its range .
some recent research conduct by Oregon State University have give considerable credence to this idea .
OSU forestry professor William Ripple and Robert Beschta have find that wolf actually promote stream - bank stabilization , although they have give the phenomenon the unfortunate name of " the ecology of fear " -- something that smack of the horrible pr result from the wolf 's relationship with Riding Hood and the Three Pigs .
they explain that elk in Yellowstone use to browse unmolested on young aspen and willow grow near the bank of stream , a behavior that prevent the sapling from reach mature stage and increase the possibility of soil erosion .
since reintroduction , however , Ripple and Beschta have find , fear of the wolf apparently have discourage the elk from spend too much time at stream bank -- where they be out in the open -- and munch on the sapling .
" all you have to do be look at the photograph , " Ed Bangs , wolf recovery coordinator for the U.S. Fish and Wildlife Service , tell UPI 's Blue Planet ,
" you say , ' wow ! '
a area that use to be bald as a billiard ball be now a sea of willow . "
this simple change have trigger a veritable ecological cascade in Yellowstone .
more streamside willow and aspen have mean better habitat for beaver , for instance .
where there have be only one beaver colony in the park 's northern range before the wolf return , now there be nine .
" it may be uninteresting to a lot of people , " Beschta tell Blue Planet .
" there be a lot of impact on plant and they say , ' who care ? '
but we have be look at streamside community .
since wolf recovery , streamside plant , willow and cottonwood provide food for other critter -- beaver , a whole variety of avian species , berry - produce shrub that bear can use .
it be important with regard to the quality of stream .
the plant provide shade and root strength for bank stability .
plant be critical to wildland ecosystem . "
Yellowstone have a vast elk herd , one of the largest in the world .
Bangs say although the number of elk have not decline very much since the wolf come back , they behavior appear markedly different .
" I be pretty suspicious of make broad generalization , " however , he caution .
" wolf be still pretty new .
they have only be there for 10 year .
in 10 more year we will have a better idea . "
wolf reintroduction in the northern Rockies have be so successful the Fish and Wildlife Service have move to reduce the animal 's status from endangered to threatened and , eventually , to remove it from the endangered species list altogether .
Bangs say the agency have establish viable wolf pack in the northern Rockies , as require by federal regulation .
some conservationist want the protection extend so wolf can move into other state , include Colorado , Utah and Oregon , among other .
on Jan. 31 , Oregon Federal District Court Judge Robert E. Jones appear to agree with they .
he vacate the FWS decision to downgrade the wolf 's status .
Bangs say he agency be still review the decision .
regardless of the wolf 's legal status , its future expansion into new area now seem likely .
wolf can migrate considerable distance .
meanwhile , he reputation seem to be improve , although Bangs note a " pretty interesting social dynamic . "
there be only about 850 wolf in the west , but there be a estimate 31,000 mountain lion .
they even occasionally attack people , which wolf do not -- despite the propaganda from the Brothers Grimm .
yet people seem willing -- even eager -- to accommodate mountain lion , despite the risk .
it remain to be see whether they will extend the same courtesy to the arrive gray wolf .
regard those rumor about wolf live in Yellowstone prior to the official reintroduction ?
they seem to be just that : rumor .
true , there be about 300,000 wolf and wolf hybrid keep as pet in the United States .
it also be likely people have release some of these animal into the wild hope they would survive -- for instance , a ranger in Glacier Park catch someone in this very act not long ago .
Bangs say these animal be not equip to survive in the wild , however , and they all almost certainly have die .
he say after 10 year of dna testing on northern Rockies wolf , scientist have not find a single strain that do not belong to one of the wolf the agency release -- or they descendant .

climate : human fuss , animal adjust
by Dan Whipple
UNITED PRESS INTERNATIONAL
Boulder , CO , Nov. 15 ( UPI ) --
scientist can argue all they want about how many degree Celsius -- or Fahrenheit -- the planet be warm and what the trend portend , but meanwhile Earth 's plant , insect and animal be not wait for the outcome .
they already be alter they pattern of behavior in response to what be happen .
it turn out one of the surest barometer of the warm climate be the response of the non-human natural world to change condition , and biologist who study the response have be aware for some year the biosphere be acknowledge global warming .
Nina Leopold Bradley , a plant ecologist and daughter of the conservation pioneer Aldo Leopold , publish a 1999 paper in the Proceedings of the National Academy of Sciences on she 61 - year uninterrupted phenological record .
phenology study a organism 's development and life cycle -- the pulse of life .
Bradley 's record of 300 phenophase find that even prior to 1999 , spring be arrive in higher latitudes several week earlier than in the earlier year of she data .
bird arrive sooner on they migration from the south and plant flower earlier .
the eastern phoebe be show up about 20 day before it use to .
the forest phlox be bloom in late April instead of mid-May .
half of the 300 phenophase Leopold track show a response consistent with warming .
in England , the cuckoo return earlier .
Pew researcher look at about 40 study that could provide a assessment of whether climate be affect biology .
" half of the study provide strong evidence of a causal link between the biological change and climate change , " say Camille Parmesan , a University of Texas - Austin biologist and one of the world 's lead expert on this issue .
these change be occur across all species , Parmesan tell UPI 's Climate .
" across the United States , the northern edge of species 's range be expand , " she say .
Parmesan have spend much of she career study the checkerspot butterfly , which migrate between Mexico and southern California .
some localize extinction already have occur across some of its habitat .
" empirical research point to climate as be a strong driver , " she say .
" there have be large number of population extinction in Mexico and southern California in area where the habitat be still acceptable . "
accord to Parmesan 's earlier study , one extinction event , for instance , be trigger when a checkerspot population migrate north prematurely , rely on a warm temperature signal , then be catch in a severe snowstorm in its northern habitat .
tree swallow be nest nine day earlier .
tropical species have move up to Florida and the Gulf Coast .
bird and butterfly watcher be see many , many new species come up from Mexico and the Caribbean . "
such consequence include shifting and , in some case , contraction of range and change in species composition within ecosystem .
the report also find alteration of ecosystem process such as carbon cycling and storage .
the Pew report coincide with the release in Iceland of the " Arctic Climate Impact Assessment . "
the ACIA -- with participation by the United States , Canada , Denmark , Finland , Iceland , Norway , the Russian Federation and Sweden -- be begin in 2000 .
" the impact of global warming be affect people now in the Arctic , " say ACIA chair Robert Corell .
" the Arctic be experience some of the most rapid and severe climate change on Earth .
the impact of climate change on the region and the globe be project to increase substantially in the year to come . "
the ACIA find arctic winter temperature have increase 4 degree to 7 degree Fahrenheit in the last 50 year and should go up about twice that much in the next 100 year .
arctic summer sea ice will decline by 50 percent by the end of the 21st century , the assessment find , with some model predict complete disappearance of summer sea ice .
" should the Arctic Ocean become ice - free in summer , it be likely that polar bear and some seal species would be drive toward extinction , " the report conclude .
as with so much climate research , not everyone agree with these dire prediction .
on the one hand , the IPN report agree " climate model generally predict that the temperature rise in the Arctic will substantially exceed the global rise .
this apply especially in the high Arctic where the ice cover be expect to diminish substantially with the effect that the surface absorption of solar radiation will greatly increase . "
on the other hand , the report think the news might not be so bad for the North Atlantic fishery .
" the impact of global warming on fish stock and fishery be hard to judge , " the IPN report say .
" a warming of the magnitude predict be more likely than not to be beneficial to the fishery of the North Atlantic . "
the important commercial species that probably would benefit from warming include cod , haddock , saithe , herring , blue whiting and several type of flatfish and crustacean -- such as the Norway lobster .
important species that probably would decline include shrimp , capelin , Greenland halibut and some variety of flatfish .
hide in this laundry list -- and in the pile of study examine by the Pew researcher -- be one of the fundamental chasm divide participant in the global warming debate .
the IPN report examine commercial fish species , but it neglect important non-commercial animal , such as seal and polar bear .
in a limited economic sense , therefore , the organization can argue warming might be a good thing .
the problem be whether one care what happen to the polar bear , checkerspot butterfly and other unconsumable .
the Pew researcher try to transcend the economic argument .
they assume a value -- unspecified -- for non-commercial species , and in do so render the warming news a bit less rosy .
this tug - of - war over calculate economic value be the one that ultimately will have to be decide by human , because animal and plant can adjust only so much .
" when dandelion have set the mark of May on Wisconsin pasture , it be time to listen for the final proof of spring , " write Aldo Leopold in " a Sand County Almanac . "
or maybe not .

attack on Iran : a loom folly
by William Rivers Pitt
t r u t h o u t | perspective
Monday 09 January 2006
the wire have be hum since before the new year with report that the Bush administration be plan a attack on Iran .
" the Bush administration be prepare its NATO ally for a possible military strike against suspect nuclear site in Iran in the New Year , accord to german media report , reinforce similar earlier suggestion in the turkish media , " report UPI on December 30th .
" the Berlin daily Der Tagesspiegel this week , " continue UPI , " quote ' NATO intelligence source ' who claim that the NATO ally have be inform that the United States be currently investigate all possibility of bring the mullah - lead regime into line , include military option .
this ' all option be open ' line have be President George W Bush 's publicly state policy throughout the past 18 month . "
a examination of the ramification of such a attack be desperately in order .
1 . blowback in Iraq
the recent election in Iraq be dominate by a amalgam of religiously fundamentalist shi'ite organization , principally the Dawa Party and the Supreme Council for Islamic Revolution in Iraq ( SCIRI ) .
both Dawa and SCIRI have umbilical connection to the fundamentalist shi'ite leadership in Iran that go back decade .
in essence , Iran now own a significant portion of the iraqi government .
should the United States undertake military action against Iran , the ramification in Iraq would be immediate and extreme .
in the first eight day of January , eighteen US troops have be kill in Iraq , compound by another twelve death from a Black Hawk helicopter crash on Saturday .
much of the violence aim at american force be come from disgruntled sunni faction that have they own militia , believe the last election be a sham , and hold little political power in the government .
if the US attack Iran , it be probable that american force - already tax by attack from sunni faction - will also face reprisal attack in Iraq from shi'ite faction loyal to Iran .
the result will be a dramatic escalation in US and civilian casualty , US force will be require to bunker themselves further into they basis , and US force will find themselves require to fight the very government they just finish help into power .
Iraq , already a seethe cauldron , will sink further into chaos .
2 . Iran 's armament
unlike Iraq , Iran have not spend the last fifteen year have its conventional force wear down by grueling sanction , repeat attack , and two american - lead war .
while Iran 's conventional army be not what it be during the heyday of the Iran - Iraq war - they armament have deteriorate and the veteran of that last war have retire - the nation enjoy substantial military strength nonetheless .
accord to a report issue by the Center for Strategic and International Studies in December of 2004 , Iran " have some 540,000 man under arm and over 350,000 reserve .
they include 120,000 Iranian Revolutionary Guards train for land and naval asymmetrical warfare .
Iran 's military also include holding of 1,613 main battle tank , 21,600 other armored fighting vehicle , 3,200 artillery weapon , 306 combat aircraft , 60 attack helicopter , 3 submarine , 59 surface combatant , and 10 amphibious ship . "
" Iran be now the only regional military power that pose a significant conventional military threat to Gulf stability , " continue the CSIS report .
" Iran have significant capability for asymmetric warfare , and pose the additional threat of proliferation .
there be considerable evidence that it be develop both a long - range missile force and a range of weapon of mass destruction .
it have never properly declare its holding of chemical weapon , and the status of its biological weapon program be unknown . "
a MILNET brief issue in February 2005 report , " due to its position astride the Persian Gulf , Iran have constantly be a threat to the gulf .
the so call ' tanker ' war in the late 1980 put Iran squarely in the bullseye of all nation seek to transport oil out of the region .
even the small navy that Iran put to sea be capable enough to harass shipping , and several case of small boat operation against oil well head in the gulf during that period make it clear small asymmetrical tactic of the iranian navy could be quite effective . "
" more concerning , " continue the MILNET brief , " be the priority place on expand and modernize its navy .
the CSIS report cite numerous area where Iran have fund modernization include the most troublesome aspect , anti-shipping cruise missile : ' Iran have obtain new anti-ship missile and missile patrol craft from China , midget submarine from North Korea , submarine from Russia , and modern mine . ' "
it be Iran 's missile armament that pose the greatest concern for american force in the gulf , especially for the US Navy .
Iran 's coast face the Persian Gulf be a loom wall of mountain that look down upon any naval force array in those water .
the gulf itself only have one exit , the Strait of Hormuz , which be also dominate by the mountainous iranian coastline .
in essence , Iran hold the high ground in the gulf .
missile battery array in those mountain could raise bloody havoc with any fleet deploy below .
of all the missile in Iran 's armament , the most dangerous be the russian - make SS - N - 22 Sunburn .
these missile be , simply , the fastest anti-ship weapon on the planet .
the Sunburn can reach Mach 3 at high altitude .
its maximum low - altitude speed be mach 2.2 , some three time faster than the american - make Harpoon .
the Sunburn take two short minute to cover its full range .
the missile 's manufacturer state that one or two missile could cripple a destroyer , and five missile could sink a 20,000 ton ship .
the Sunburn be also superior to the Exocet missile .
recall that it be two Exocets that rip the USS Stark to shred in 1987 , kill 37 sailor .
the Stark could not see they to stop they .
the US aircraft carrier Theodore Roosevelt be currently deploy in the Persian Gulf , with some 7,000 soul aboard .
sail with the Roosevelt be the Tarawa Expeditionary Strike Force , which include the USS Tarawa , the USS Austin , and the USS Pearl Harbor .
the USS Austin be likewise deploy in the gulf .
the Sunburn missile , with its incredible speed and ability to avoid radar detection , would do terrible damage these ship if Iran choose to retaliate in the gulf after a american attack within its border .
beyond the naval threat be the possibility of Iran throw its military muscle into the ongoing struggle in Iraq .
currently , the US be face a asymmetrical attack from group wield small arm , shoulder - fire grenade and roadside bomb .
the vaunted american military have suffer 2,210 death and ten of thousand of wounded from this form of warfare .
the occupation of Iraq have become a guerrilla war , a siege that have last more than a thousand day .
if Iran decide to throw any or all of its 23,000 armored fighting vehicle , along with any or all of its nearly million - strong army , into the Iraq fray , the situation in the Middle East could become unspeakably dire .
3 . the syrian connection
in February of 2005 , Iran and Syria agree upon a mutual protection pact to combat " challenge and threat " in the region .
a attack on Iran would trigger this mutual defense pact , and could conceivably bring Syria into direct conflict with american force .
like Iran , Syria 's military be nothing to scoff at .
virtually every credible analysis have Syria stand as the strongest military force in the Middle East after Israel .
Damascus have be intent for year upon establish significant military strength to serve as a counterweight to Israel 's overwhelming capability .
as of 2002 , Syria have some 215,000 soldier under arm , 4,700 tank , and a massive artillery capability .
the syrian Air Force be comprise of ten to eleven fighter / attack squadron and sixteen fighter squadron , total somewhere near 650 aircraft .
Syria also possess one of the largest arsenal of ballistic missile in the region , comprise primarily of SCUD - derive system .
Iran , North Korea and China have be willing provider of state - of - the - art technology .
compound this be the well - base suspicion that Syria have perhaps the most advanced chemical weapon capability in the Persian Gulf .
4 . China and the US economy
while the ominous possibility of heighten iraqi chaos , missile in the gulf , and syrian involvement loom large if the US attack Iran , all pale in comparison to the involvement of China in any US / Iran engagement .
China 's economy be explode , hamper only by they great thirst for petroleum and natural gas to fuel they industry .
China will purchase 250 million ton of liquefy natural gas from Iran over the next 30 year , will develop the massive Yadavaran oil field in Iran , and will receive 150,000 barrel of oil per day from that field .
China be seek the construction of a pipeline from Iran to the Caspian Sea , where it would link with another plan pipeline run from Kazakhstan to China .
any US attack on Iran could be perceive by China as a direct threat to its economic health .
further , any fighting in the Persian Gulf would imperil the tanker run China 's liquefy natural gas through the Strait of Hormuz .
should China decide to retaliate against the US to defend its oil and natural gas deal with Iran , the US would be face with a significant threat .
this threat exist not merely on a military level , though China could force a confrontation in the Pacific by way of Taiwan .
more significantly , China hold a large portion of the american economy in the palm of its hand .
Paul Craig Roberts , write for the American Conservative , say in July of 2005 that " as a result of many year of persistent trade surplus with the United States , the japanese government hold dollar reserve of approximately $ 1 trillion .
China 's accumulation of dollar be approximately $ 600 billion .
South Korea hold about $ 200 billion .
these sum give these country enormous leverage over the United States .
by dump some portion of they reserve , these country could put the dollar under intense pressure and send U.S. interest rate skyrocket .
Washington would really have to anger Japan and Korea to provoke such action , but in a showdown with China - over Taiwan , for example - China hold the card .
China and Japan , and the world at large , have more dollar reserve than they require .
they would have no problem teach a hegemonic superpower a lesson if the need arise . "
" the hardest blow on Americans , " conclude Roberts , " will fall when China do revalue its currency .
when China 's currency cease to be undervalue , american shopper in Wal - Mart , where 70 percent of the goods on the shelf be make in China , will think they be in Neiman Marcus .
price increase will cause a dramatic reduction in american real income .
if this coincide with rise interest rate and a setback in the housing market , american consumer will experience the hardest time since the Great Depression . "
in short , China have the american economy by the throat .
should they decide to squeeze , we will all feel it .
China 's strong hand in this even extend to the diplomatic realm ; China be a permanent member of the United Nations Security Council , and could veto any action against Iran propose by the United States .
5 . american preparedness
american citizen have for decade take it as a given that we military can overwhelm and overcome any foe on the battlefield .
the rapid victory during the first Gulf War cement this perception .
the last three year of the Iraq occupation , however , have sap this confidence .
worse , the occupation have do great damage to the strength of the american military , justify the decrease in confidence .
thanks to repeat deployment to Iraq and Afghanistan , recruiting be at a all - time low .
soldier with vital training and know - how be refuse to re-enlist .
across the board , the american military be stretch to the breaking point .
two vaunted economist - one a Nobel Prize winner and the other a nationally renowned budget expert - have analyze the data at hand and put a price tag on the Iraq occupation .
accord to Linda Bilmes of Harvard and Nobel Laureate Joseph E. Stiglitz of Columbia University , the final cost of the Iraq occupation will run between $ 1 trillion and $ 2 trillion , surpass by order of magnitude the estimate put forth by the Bush administration .
if a engagement with Iran envelop we force in Iraq , and come to involve Syria , we economy will likely shatter under the strain of fight so many country simultaneously .
add to this the economic threat pose by China , and the economic threat implicit in any substantial disruption of the distribution of Mideast petroleum to the globe .
if Iran and Syria - with they significant armament , missile technology and suspect chemical weapon capability - decide to engage with the relatively undersized US force in Iraq , we troops there will be fish in a barrel .
Iran 's position over the gulf would make resupply by ship and air support from carrier a dangerous affair .
in the worst - case scenario , the newly - mint american order of battle require the use of nuclear weapon to rescue a surround and imperil force could come into play , hurl the entire planet into military and diplomatic bedlam .
conclusion : be any of this possible ?
it be difficult to imagine a justification for any action that could envelop the United States in a military and economic conflict with Iraq , Iran , Syria and China simultaneously .
Iran be suspect by many nation of work towards the development of nuclear weapon , but even this justification have be toss into a cocked hat .
recently , russian president Vladimir Putin bluntly state that Iran be not develop its nuclear capability for any reason beyond peaceful energy creation , and pledge to continue assist Iran in this endeavor .
therefore , any attack upon Iran 's nuclear facility will bring Russia into the mess .
Iran also stand accuse of aid terrorism across the globe .
the danger implicit in any attack upon that nation , however , seem to significantly offset whatever gain could be make in the so - call " war on terror . "
unfortunately , all the danger in the world be no match for the self - assurance of a bubble - encase zealot .
what manner of maniac would undertake such a dangerous course ?
look no further than 1600 Pennsylvania Avenue .
George W. Bush and he administration have consistently undertake incredibly dangerous course of action in order to garner political power on the home front .
recall the multiple terror threat lob out by the administration whenever damaging political news appear in the media .
more significantly , recall Iraq .
Karl Rove , Bush 's most senior advisor , notoriously tell Republicans on the ballot during the 2002 midterm to " run on the war . "
the invasion of Iraq provide marvelous political cover for the GOP not only during those midterm , but during the 2004 presidential election .
what kind of political cover would be gain from a attack on Iran , and from the diversion of attention to that attack ?
the answer lie in one now - familiar name : Jack Abramoff .
the Abramoff scandal threaten to subsume all the hard - fight GOP gain in Congress , and the 2006 midterm be less than a year away .
be any of this a probability ?
logic say no , but logic seldom play any part in modern american politics .
all argument that the Bush administration would be insane to attack Iran and risk a global conflagration for the sake of political cover run into one unavoidable truth .
they do it once already in Iraq .

I have a splitter / filter between my adsl and ph line ?
I have 2 phone run on the same line and the adsl which be connect to one of the phone and the filter , I be still get a buzzing noise even when I have disconnect the other phone without one .
why be it stil do this even though I do not have the other phone connect ?
would it be better if I get another filter and connect the other phone as well ?
turn the modem off and see if the sound be still there ... could be static on the line ... if the sound be still there with the modem off then the problem be not the dsl ....
if the trouble go away with the modem off , then make sure that everything except the modem be filter , this would include the alarm system , fax machine , satellite box , phone , etc ...
if everything be filter , and you still have this problem - try change the filter - if it be still there , try double up on the filter ...
you need either a filter for each device except the dsl modem , or a whole home filter which filter all the jack , except the one which the dsl modem connect .

hamster - will a hamster be ok live in the bathroom ?
in he cage in the bathroom ?
or would the steam from the shower be a problem ?
if space be minimal , or you be keep he in there to be keep away from other pet , then I can understand why you would choose to keep he there .
there be some thing to consider though ...
rodent require special bedding in they cage to absorb they waste , and this need to be clean regularly , or you hamster could suffer from problem due the buildup of ammonia from he urine .
when you take a warm shower and build up steam , he cage will collect water , the bedding will absorb much of it , and will not be able to absorb the urine quite as it should .
you will also have to be wary of mold form on any toy or hide - away he may have .
you also do not want it get too warm for he too often .
overall , it be not a good solution , but you can keep he healthy and pull it off if you take the time to give he the extra care he will need because of it .
it may be a problem because the temperature be constantly change .
I would personally put he somewhere else .

how do i get to paris cdg airport to paris montparnasse ?
i have two option
use the metro or the air france bus
can anybody tell I if the metro run directly from CDG to montparnasse ?
in the airport , follow the sign that say " Paris by train " .
buy a ticket for Paris .
this will get you on the RER b line go into town .
stay on it until the " Saint - Michel Notre - Dame " station .
change there to the Metro 4 line go toward " Porte d' Orleans " .
get off at the " Montparnasse Bienvenue " station .
on the Air France bus :
as I recall , this bus drop you off near the Opera in Paris .
you will still have to take another bus or the Metro down to Montparnasse .
on the bus : get on bus 95 go toward " Porte de Vanves " .
buy a ticket from the driver .
stay on the bus until the " Montparnasse Bienvenue " stop .
on the Metro : get in the Metro at Opera .
take the 8 line toward " Balard " until the " Invalides " station .
change there to the 13 line toward " Chatillon Montrouge " and take it until the " Montparnasse Bienvenue " station .

you could also try this in gimp .
it will give you a lot more power , as well as control over how you black and white photo look :
open you image while it be still in color
create a new layer and fill the later with black .
set the layer mode to " color " this will make you image blak and white .
click color >>> level and adjust each channel 's color value .
this will adjust the brightness and darkness of specific part of a image .
for more information on the theory behind later mode check out this gimp video tutorial : http://gimpedblog.blogspot.com/2011/09/gimp-video-tutorial-how-to-convert.html
for more information on adjust exposure in gimp chef out this gimp video tutorial : http://gimpedblog.blogspot.com/2011/09/how-to-use-gimp-for-beginners-lesson-4.html
hope this help .

how to start a new fish tank ?
I be get a 10 gallon for my betta tomorrow and I just want to know how to properly set it up .
I be still a beginner .
any and all suggestion on what I need to do and buy will help .
when you get the tank make sure you wash the inside ( with plain water ) then you wash the gravel ( with only water too ) take out all the stuff that be float on top .
add only silk plant as plastic one may tear up ur betta 's delicate fin .
you add the water and put water conditioner into the water .
start up you filter ( sponge filter be the best for betta ) and put in a heater and set it to anywhere between 78 - 82 .
wait about 2 week or 3 and test you water .
if everything be look good you may add you betta to its new home .
light be optinal since fish need the light turn off at night anyways and a air pump be not nessasary since they get air from the surface .
ask the people sell you the fish how you should set it up , they would know
add aquasafe with the water you put in it .
make sure the temperature be good .
do not put you fish tank close to the sun or alga grow in you tank .
everything else should be good .
make sure if you get new fish that they get along with one another .

question about the sinking of the Titanic ?
after the sinking of the Titanic in 1912 , be there a law make so that ship would carry enough lifeboat to save everybody on a ship if it be sink ?
sorry , I be just very nervous after watch the movie .
SOLAS ( Safety of Life at Sea ) , which be a international maritime treaty , come about in response to the tragedy of the Titanic .
today , it be the primary safety law affect virtually all ship , regardless of country of registration .
most ship perform this drill before even leave the dock .
SOLAS cover just about every aspect of safety at sea , include minimum safety equipment , practice , and standard , lifeboat , navigation practice , fire protection , and so on .
we be much safer today on board ship due to SOLAS , and I suppose if any good come out of the Titanic tragedy , the adoption of SOLAS be probably it .
edit : also I forget to mention earlier , most ( if not all ) cruise ship also practice lifeboat drill weekly , and it be not uncommon to see they to actually launch the lifeboat into the water as part of they drill when you be in port .
this not only ensure the lifeboat be operational and will work if need , but make the crew proficient at launch they .
I do not think so
do not worry .
when be the last time you hear about a ship sink ?

but I would go for the base number of 15 hh .

where in the world be Iguazu ?
the centre of the falls be know locally as ' Garganta Del Diablo ' ( the Devil 's Throat ) , where the huge volume of water send a constant mist of spray into the air .
with the sun shin down on the spray , create a rainbow in the foreground , this be the perfect place to get that trademark Iguazu Falls photograph .
however , save some of you shot for the rest of the fall , as in total there be around 270 cascade that spread out over nearly 2 mile of the Iguazu River .
the Iguazu Falls be easily accessible and , dependent on you time restriction and budget , you can get to the area by either bus or plane .
the nearest town to the site be Puerto Iguazu in Argentina , about 12 mile from the falls , and Foz do Iguaçu in Brazil , which be equally close .
both town have airport that be serve regularly from the larger city such as Sao Paulo , Rio de Janeiro and Buenos Aires .
the bus be obviously the cheaper option , and travel up from Buenos Aires the trip be a full 20 hour , although the bus be very comfortable with spacious recline seat .
the bus trip down from Sao Paulo be a similar affair take around 18 hour .
Foz on the brazilian side be the larger town , however both be gear up to cater for visitor to the waterfall and national park , and so offer a range of accommodation for all budget .
for those with a larger appetite for the scenery and a larger budget , there be some hotel complex much closer to the action with view of part of the fall .

what be italian high Renaissance ?
have a look at this , it may help .
1 ) the Italian Renaissance begin the opening phase of the Renaissance , a period of great cultural change and achievement in Europe that span the period from the end of the 13th century to about 1600 , mark the transition between medieval and early modern Europe .
the term renaissance be in essence a modern one that come into currency in the 19th century , in the work of historian such as Jacob Burckhardt .
although the origin of a movement that be confine largely to the literate culture of intellectual endeavor and patronage can be trace to the earlier part of the 14th century , many aspect of italian culture and society remain largely medieval ; the Renaissance do not come into full swing until the end of the century .
the word renaissance ( Rinascimento in Italian ) mean " rebirth " , and the era be best know for the renew interest in the culture of classical antiquity after the period that Renaissance humanist label the Dark Ages .
these change , while significant , be concentrate in the elite , and for the vast majority of the population life be little change from the Middle Ages .
this term be first use in German ( hochrenaissance ) in the early nineteenth century , and have its origin in the " high style " of painting and sculpture describe by Johann Joachim Winckelmann .
[ 1 ] over the last twenty year , use of the term have be frequently criticize by academic art historian for over-simplify artistic development , ignore historical context , and focus only on a few iconic work .
[ 2 ]

what would you get if you cross a sussex male and a silkie female ?
i have a sussex male and a pekin female i buy 2 silky what would the sussex female and the silkie female would make ?
if you have any pic of you hen i would like to see they to compare they to mine thanks ?
a sussex cross with silkie would make a crossbreed * mutt * chicken .
there be a lot of genetics at play between a sussex and silkie , so the offspring would vary in appearance .
however , I can say what feature they would / could have .
feather type .
silky have hookless feather .
sussex have soft feather .
all offspring from this cross will have soft feather , as hookless feather be a recessive gene .
skin Color : silky have black skin color , which be dominate .
sussex have white skin which could be recessive or dominate .
either way rec. and dom. white gene dilute the black gene .
skin will be darker but lighter than the silky .
beard / muff : if you silkie have a beard / muff the offspring could have a beard as well , as these gene be incomplete dominate .
feathered foot / shank - chick could have feathered foot / shank as this be also incomplete dominate .
crest : chick could also develop a small crest due to this be another incomplete dominate gene .
comb type : silky have walnut comb which be actually genetically two comb type ( rose and pea ) single be also there , but be recessive .
so cross to a Sussex you could get a walnut , pea , rose , or single comb bird .
five toe : silky have five toe .
sussex have four toe .
cross together ( five toe be incompletely dominate ) chick could develop to have a fifth toe on both , or even one foot .
silkie cross be great bird , and very neat look .
hen make excellent mother as they be bigger , can see better , and be smarter than silky .
best wish ,
Jamie / RhodeRunner

what be some unique custom in ireland ?
as far as I be aware we most unique custom would be the " country wake " .
in all my travels I have never see anything like it and be often meet with a odd look when I explain they to foreigner .
in this time visitor will come to the house , pay they respects to the desisted and they family and have a couple of cup of tea with a sandwich or a bun .
the wake also include the night sit were friend and family sit up through the night with the remains .
wake be common both north and south of the boarder with Protestants and Catholics alike .
but only really in the countryside .
the only notable difference I have notice be that in the south of Ireland one night of the wake be often hold in the chapel the night before the funeral , this tradition start after the civil war .

pewter be perfect for what you be do , and it melt on a stove top .
I would recommend to start with something more simple like tin , pewter , aluminum or zinc , they all have a much more reasonable melting point .

ok so if your snake will take pre-killed , you can " gas it " .
just put the rat in a seal tupperware container with no airhole and wait until it pass out and die and then feed it .
if it will not take pre-killed and you usually feed live then you could hold the rat by the tail and whack it against a hard surface , like a refrigerator or wall .
I do not like that option though - I think it be pretty cruel and if not do properly you will end up really hurt the rat but not stun he enough to stop possible injury to you snake .
I would do the tupperwear idea tbh - easiest and most humane .
you could also just wait until the rat pass out for about 1 minute and them feed it - at this point , it could still have a bit of a heart beat and be slightly still alive .
and also maybe try hold the rat in feeding prong so you snake can get a good hold and grip on he prey .
good luck !
just my opinion here - no judgement - get you snake on freeze / thaw will prove to be much easier for you and safer for you snake in the long run .
my opinion - take it for what it be worth . :-)

hi , I be a dog trainer for 25 yr .
you need to purchase what be call a shoulder point harness .
this type of harness go around the dog 's chest and leg and have a clip for the leash up on the back of the dog in middle of shoulder blade .
this way , he can not reach the leash to chew it .
when he swivel he head to go for it anyway , tell he sharp " uh uh " gently correct he with a small tug and continue you walk .
do this repeatedly and frequently and he will learn to walk on a leash .
patience be the key here .
he be a young pup and will learn over time and consistency in he training .
and always , always train with love and positive method - never hit or harshly scold .
never train out of fear .
you want you dog to admire you as he pack leader , not fear you .
good luck with you puppy !
all the best .

they be social and like to be handle .
you have to have two because they do not do well alone .
make certain you get two female .
two male can fight and you definitely do not want baby !!
guinea pig ( also call cavy ) be gentle creature and be awake during the day and sleep at night .
they will whistle when they hear you as a encouragement for you to give they a treat like leaf lettuce .
they love leaf or romaine lettuce and tomato , celery , cucumber , carrot .
do not feed they broccoli , cauliflower , garlic , onion , head lettuce .... they be all too difficult for they to digest .
also they can not eat potato , they be toxic for they .
if you keep the cage clean they do not smell and you can buy spray on cleaser for they , just massage it into they coat and groom they .

what be the requirement to apply for a delay birth certificate in canada ?
what be the evidentary requirement to apply for a delay birth certificate in canada ?
include fee and form
it depend on if you ever register the birth .
some place do the registration right at the hospital .... in some smaller place , you need to register you child 's birth at the town hall / registrar 's office .
my first three child be bear in southern Ontario city .
the birth registration be do right in hospital .
my last son , be bear in northern Ontario ....
I do not know that I do not register he in the ridiculous amount of paperwork I have fill out in the hospital and be suppose to go to city hall within 90 day .
two year later when I get around to fill for he birth certificate , I find out he be never register .
I have to call the Office of the Registrar General in Thunder Bay , have copy of the delayed registration form mail out to I , as they do not have a online area for it yet , fill those out , send they away , then apply for he birth certificate .
if you be just apply for a birth certificate for the first time , it be simple to do it over the computer .
for $ 56 you can even have it expedite and will get in three business day or you money back .
this be in Ontario of course , the rate may be slightly different for other province / territory .
none , just walk in to the service office and present all the identification you have to prove you identity .
they may then choose to ask you to bring more evidence , or just look up the record and hand you the certificate .
you can probably do it all on - line .
start here if you be bear in Ontario .
if you be bear elsewhere , start here .
my parent do not send for my birth certificate until I be 16 and need it for summer employment .
it be no problem to get provide the birth be register in the first place .
I add that in because there have be some people who have try to claim citizenship by send for they birth certificate when they be never really bear in Canada or to canadian parent .
when a child be bear in Canada the birth be register before the baby can leave the hospital .
as long as that be do you can send for it at any time .
each provincial government have a website that list the process for that Province so depend upon where you be bear you can google it .

how do you make you cat adjust to a new house ?
I and my family be move into a new house just outside a small town .
we be currently live a mile from the town in a house surround by field but the new house be beside a busy road .
we have have the cat for 10 year and do not want to leave it .
how could we make it settle in a new house .
you be not just move house - you cat be lose he territory .
you will need to give he only a small place to explore , so he can make it he territory , and feel safe there .
then , he can have a place to retreat to when he feel scared .
you will need to get he box and bowl , and whatever blanket and toy be he , and smell like home , and put he in a room .
close the door , and keep he in there for a week .
he will feel much safer in that one room , than in a huge unknown house .
he will explore the room , mark everything with he cheek , and try to make it feel like he territory .
he will reassure himself that no other animal be in there , and that no other animal will come in - he be afraid that he be in someone else 's territory when he be in a new house .
in a week 's time , he will have make it he , and will be get more bored than afraid .
let he out for half a hour , to explore .
then put he back in .
he will be freak out , so go back to he territory will make he much happier .
extend the time he be out each day , but for the first month , always put he in he room at night , so he feel safe to sleep .
soon he will make the whole house he , but he need that one safe place to start from .
remember to visit with he while he be in the room , and tell he how good he be .
remember to give he the time he need to feel that the room be he - rush it , and he will be afraid of the whole house for a long time .
he might even start pee on thing in fear .
good luck with you new house and with he new territory !
let she explore when we move my cat have to explore the entire house before she feel comfortable .
in time though she / he will adjust . :)
they just do it on they own .

remember snake can go a while without eat .
in the winter , they will usually go deep underground and enter a hibernation - like state call brumation , which be characterize by a slowed metabolism and reduce activity .
king snake sometimes stop eat , particularly during the cooler part of the year .
they have a natural instinct to hibernate .
if the snake be not pregnant or shed , and its enclosure be properly equip , a loss of appetite probably signal a beginning of hibernation .
hibernation be natural , and a necessity for snake that be go to be breed .
another thing that can cause a king snake to stop eat be shedding .
you can tell when you king snake be about to shed , because its eye will get milky look .
its body will be dull look , too .
in a few day the snake will begin to shed its skin .
for example , some snake will routinely go off they food in both the summer and winter , feed mainly in spring and fall .
it be natural and so long as you do not see any serious deterioration in they health be nothing to worry about .
you see , some snake for no obvious reason will simply go off they food .
they be fit and healthy and they care be suitable .

bearded dragon question ... ?
I just buy a baby one yesterday .

I have bearded dragon juvenile food and freeze - dry cricket .

uvb on the other hand can only be reproduce by a fluorescent source .
uvb will always be a separate bulb from the heat lamp , unless you use a mvb ( mercury vapor bulb ) which be the only reptile use bulb that will emit both uvb and heat from one bulb .
I highly recommend that you do not use coiled / compact uvb bulb as they be know to cause severe eye damage and / or blindness in reptile not to mention they have trouble maintain uvb output over time .
the long tube uvb bulb be best , like Zoomed 's Repsitun model : http://lllreptile.com/store/catalog/reptile-supplies/uvb-fluorescent-lights-mercury-vapor-bulbs/-/zoo-med-24-repti-sun-100-fluorescent-bulb/ remember to replace uvb bulb accord to the manufacturer 's recommendation after which time the bulb will no longer produce uvb even if visible light still be .
so , to answer you question , no , if you just have a bulb that say it produce UVA then you do not have " the sun 's ray " that you beard need .
you need to also provide a source of UVB lighting .
the person at Petsmart be very wrong ; in fact it be always a good idea to second guess what most pet store employee tell you ; they do not have the best track record regard give reliable pet care info .
UVB and bask temp ( should be about 110 F for a baby , 95 F for a adult ) should be available for 10 - 12 hour a day .
freeze dry food be not a good staple food source ; you need to offer live feeder insect .
bearded dragon be sight hunter , they need to see the food move to trigger a feed response , especially when they be baby .
Live food be also higher in nutritional value than freeze dried .
cricket , silk worm , phoenix worm , and various feeder roach , like red - lobster , turkistan , and dubia , be good example of staple insect to offer you beard .
Wax worm and meal worm should only be offer as treat item , for variety 's sake .
I would highly recommend that you read through some reliable beard guide to make sure you have everything set up correctly :
either way you also need to keep a eye on the temperature if you be use a dry fish tank as UV light in my experience up the temperature significantly and without proper ventilation it can become a oven .
that lady at PetSmart be a disgrace to the rest of we PetSmart associate ... sheesh .
yes , it give he the " sun ray " necessary , that be what UVA be .
and it should be on 10 - 12 hour , just like the sun would be up for 10 - 12 hour in he natural environment .
as for the heat , just be sure to use a thermometer .
I tell all my customer they can try it , but do not count on it .
also try green leafy veggy , like kale and spinach .
best of luck !

people do not go to Ireland on holiday for the weather , it be unpredictable .
one thing you can be sure of about irish weather be how little you can be sure of .
it may be shirtsleeve and sunglass in February , but winter woolly in March and even during the summer .
County Kerry be the worst affect .
the southeast be the driest , enjoy a more continental climate .
the irish weather work on the ' four season in a day ' principle , which basically mean that you can not predict a thing when it come to the behaviour of the sky .
some basic assumption , however , can be make .
it be also peak tourist season , which mean there be far more people just about everywhere but the most remote corner of the island , and price be at they highest .
not surprisingly , most of the yearly festival occur during these time so as to take advantage of the crowd and the more favourable weather .
spring ( February to April ) and Autumn ( August to October ) make good alternative , although the country 's ever - grow popularity as a tourist destination can often blur the line between mid - and high - season tourism .
still , you have a better chance of some peace and quiet , and the weather can be surprisingly better in April and September than in mid-July - again , it be all part of the uncertainty principle .
Spring festivity include the ever - popular St Patrick 's Festival .
although temperature do not often venture below freezing , winter ( December to February ) can be brutal , for huge part of the country - the west and northwest in particular .
crowd be at they thinnest , but many of the country 's tourist attraction and service close down in October and do not reopen until Easter , which paradoxically leave visitor with a more convincing taste of how Ireland be experience by most of the irish : it be cold , grey and dark by 5 pm , but there be always a pub to escape into when the rain start sheet down .
as that famous Scotsman Billy Connolly say " there be no such thing as bad weather just the wrong clothes "
afraid I can not be more helpful , it be really a case of pot luck , although as the weather be so changeable often a cold wet morning will turn into a lovely warm sunny afternoon and evening or visa versa .

if they be able to take earthworm uncut , that be really impressive !
I aspire to you feeding regime , flake early and something live later in the day .
worm ( and daphnia ) be also rich in lipid , substance important in form egg and grow young .
I think that you understand that you largest and smallest golden wonder be male .
if you would like more on sex out Aplocheilus lineatus take a look at the discussion in the first source below .
if you have plant in you tank .
you lineatus be already spawn .
if condition be favorable ( 78 - 82 f ) and the fish be obviously well feed as yours be , they will spawn .
( I have even have a pair of killy leave egg on a float thermometer !
if you wish to pick egg make a acrylic spawning mop .
check out the second source .
I prefer darker color because I can see they egg , more easily and the fish look better next to they .
use a well rinse medicine vial , a cork , new fishing bobber or even a piece of non-crumbly styrofoam to float they .
there be a couple way one could spawn lineatus - mop spawn & water incubate they for two week , pick egg from a mop & put they in a tray of treated , seasoned water or set up the parent in a plant tank & move they so the fry can hatch out there .
if you have the room to separate the male ( s ) & female ( s ) , & feed they well on live food , ( assume that you be do weekly 50 % water change ) when you put they together they will leave a lot more egg .
just make up example , but if a pair be constantly together , they may lay 10 - 15 egg a day .
with extra blackworm and maybe freeze ( defrost , rinse ) freeze food earlier in the day , they may leave 30 - 40 egg at a time .
separate and feed extremely nourishing stuff , they may produce more .
separate a pair some time before a show ( killy be usually show & judge & often sell as pair ) will encourage they to court and show they best color .
they also start the day with no nick or ding in they fin .
the water change help with that too .
you also may need to treat the incubation water .
the chlorine and ammonia ( choramine ) be not good for the egg .
ironically sometimes it be wise to leave the newly pick egg in fresh tap water with some chlorination to kill microscopic critter that ride in with the egg .
then put the egg in water treat a couple of day before with a water treatment and leave open to " breathe " .
leave a jar with a dozen black worm in it will sate the adult 's desire for snack and they be more likely to leave fry or egg alone .
if a pair be not leave egg ... check the follow :
1 . be a tank mate ( such as another female killie or a cory or large snail ) rate the egg ?
2 . have we keep up with partial water change ?
3 . be there too much mineral in the water ?
aplo. lineatus be wide - spread over southern India .
that indicate that they thrive in different water chemistry .
still if you can get you pet shop to do a hardness or tds ( total dissolve solid ) test , that may give you a hint .
wing it a little here , a hardness of 100 to nearly 200 ppm ( part per million ) or 5.8 to 10.6 dh should be fine for gardnerus .
tds meter ( the thrifty aquarist 's hardness meter can be use if one have see one of you municipal water department 's annual report .
they include a number of mineral there and you can figure out what percentage of that would be you hardness mineral ( calcium , magnesium and iron ) .
a number of mineral be not of much consequence .
however if there be a high level of sodium chloride ( common salt ) that can break down the chorion ( shell ) around the egg and allow critter to get in and eat the yoke and embryo . )
ironically sometimes it be wise to newly pick egg in fresh tap water with some chlorination to kill microscopic critter that ride in with the egg .
then put the egg in water treat a couple of day before with a water treatment and leave open to " breathe " .
if you get egg in the mail in a medicine vial , that be fine .
but get the egg out , maybe rinse in fresh tap water and then into the incubation water .
in time the egg can suffocate in the shipping container .
after a number of people begin complain about " mystery death " among incubate egg , some of the more advanced killie people begin suggest that after 7 - 8 day of incubation , one should do a 100 % water change - as the egg develop , they do release waste material .
another problem be that sometimes bad egg will fungus and the fungus will spread out and kill all the egg .
some people put in a very dilute Acriflaven solution to slow down the fungus , so one can take white egg out with a pipette or eyedropper .
other will add a drop of Methylene blue .
if a egg turn blue , it have die and then become dyed as the outer membrane break down .
get those out asap too .
hope there be useful grist for the mill here .

well it take we a while to find one that we like .
but we do not just like house of Joy we love it .
everything we have get there have be more authentic and better taste than any other chinese restaurant in the San Antonio area we have be to -- and trust I we have be to a lot of they .
we just happen to stumble across this little restaurant one day when we have to visit the Bexar County Tax Office off of Bandera Road .
we stop in and get some take out and can not stop go back .
they have the best Egg Drop Soup I have ever taste .
we also love they egg roll and spring roll .
and every entree we have order be perfect .
everything be always cook fresh and taste fresh .
they price be extremely reasonable for the amount of food you receive .
the staff be also just so pleasant to deal with .
they be also quick at get you order out to you .
you do not have to sit and wait around forever like most place !!
so anyone look for a excellent night out for chinese or maybe just lunch should stop in and try it because I promise you 2 thing --- you will not regret it !!
and you will go back for more !!!
Karla Ferguson - Granger

we be from Virginia and just move here a year ago .
so that comment be completely false .
because we think it be the best !!!
and we do not know they except for eat there .
